# CLAUDE.md — handoff to Claude Code

> **Read this first.** This file is for Claude Code agents picking up work
> on skateOS. The full project memory + working rules + every decision so
> far live in `MEMORY.md` — read that next.

## What this project is
**skateOS** — operating system for skate parks. White-label product, first deployment is **2nd Nature Park** (Peekskill, NY). Single-page admin SPA + Supabase + Expo mobile. Forked from Smart Lawn NY admin on Apr 16, 2026.

Owner: Doug Brown + Jon DiCarlo (50/50). Email: info@2ntr.com.

## Read these files in order before doing anything
1. **`MEMORY.md`** — all working rules, account scope, active projects, accounts, in-progress notes. The single source of truth on Doug's working preferences.
2. **`README.md`** — project architecture overview.
3. **`RUNBOOK.md`** — auth, backups, payments, secrets, outage procedures.
4. **`AUDIT.md`** — Smart Lawn leftover strings, broken handlers, what's working vs not, status of every module.
5. **`SKATEOS_VS_SQUARE.md`** — feature scope, what we build vs skip, post-MVP priority list.
6. **`SMARTLAWN_PATTERNS.md`** — what's borrowable from the parent Smart Lawn codebase at `/Volumes/LaCie/Lawn/Claude-smartlawnny.com/`.
7. **`ORGANIZATION.md`** (in `~/Desktop/Skate/`) — file organization status, pending Phase 2 restructure.

## Working rules (the ones Doug enforces hardest)
- **Do, don't ask.** Anytime Claude can do it itself, do it. Reserve questions for things only Doug can do (logins, billing, irreversible product calls).
- **Claude is the assistant, NOT the boss.** Doug sets direction; Claude executes.
- **Never be idle.** Either doing work or asking exactly one focused question.
- **Always show real artifacts each turn**, not announcements of artifacts.
- **Background mode:** when nothing's been asked for, keep going on the next-priority TODO.
- **End with a "what's next" list** when paused for input.
- **Branch Manager / Smart Lawn = reference-only.** Read patterns, write skate-shaped equivalents in this repo. Never `import`, never copy whole files.

## Session log — 2026-05-18 (Netlify → Cloudflare migration)

Netlify team paused for credit-limit overage → all 3 sites 404. Doug: "if i havent paid yet and we can migrate now? how long til it will work. why not just switch?" Picked Cloudflare Pages over paying $19/mo Netlify Pro.

| Surface | Deliverable |
|---|---|
| GitHub repo | `github.com/skatepark914/skateOS` created + initial push (464 objects, 2.76 MiB). `.gitignore` written to exclude `.DS_Store`, `.netlify/`, `.wrangler/`, `node_modules/`, `*-dist/`, `.env*`. Repo description set + homepage URL set to skateos.com. |
| `marketing/wrangler.jsonc` | New Cloudflare Workers static-assets config. `assets.directory = "."`, `not_found_handling = "404-page"`. Two `custom_domain` routes: `skateos.com` + `www.skateos.com`. `workers_dev = true` keeps the .workers.dev fallback URL alive for testing. |
| `marketing/.assetsignore` | Excludes `.wrangler/**`, `.netlify/**`, `*.md`, build artifacts from public deploy. |
| `admin/wrangler.jsonc` | Same model but `not_found_handling = "single-page-application"` so unknown routes serve `index.html` (SPA routing works). One `custom_domain` route: `app.skateos.com`. |
| `admin/.assetsignore` | Excludes `migrations/**`, `scripts/**`, `*.sh`, `*.bak`, `*.md` so SQL migrations + provisioning scripts aren't publicly served. |
| GoDaddy nameservers | Already swapped to Cloudflare (`cheryl.ns.cloudflare.com` / `jakub.ns.cloudflare.com`) on 2026-05-06, discovered via `GET /zones?name=skateos.com`. No DNS work needed. |
| Deploy commands | `cd marketing && npx wrangler deploy` and `cd admin && npx wrangler deploy`. Replace the old `netlify deploy` commands in DOUG-TODO.md + TUTORIAL.md. |
| Smoke test | 9 URLs return 200 — `skateos.com`, `www.skateos.com`, `skateos.com/{locked,2ntr,sales}`, `app.skateos.com`, `app.skateos.com/join`, both `.workers.dev` fallbacks. |

### Doug to do

1. **Confirm admin login works** — open `https://app.skateos.com` → sign in → verify Supabase auth + data loads
2. **Cancel Netlify upgrade plan** (if you started one) — Cloudflare Workers free tier covers this load forever
3. **Marketing on Netlify is dead** — both old projects (`skateos` `2c6535a3-...` + `skateos-app` `b46cf6b7-...`) can be deleted from Netlify dashboard once you've verified Cloudflare works

## Session log — 2026-05-15 capstone (Per-tenant Brivo webhook URLs)

Doug: _"yes, ALWAYS KEEP GOING WHEN MAKES SENSE it in your memory"_ — saved the directive to memory + kept building.

| Surface | Deliverable |
|---|---|
| `brivo-webhook` | Added explicit-tenant routing via `?tenant=<uuid>` query param OR `x-skateos-tenant` header. New signature-verification resolution order: (0) explicit tenant → that tenant's secret, (1) env var, (2) customer-lookup fallback, (3) reject. Multi-tenant installs can now skip the dual-attempt fallback dance by giving each park their own per-tenant URL. |
| Settings → Brivo per-tenant credentials | New "🔗 PER-TENANT WEBHOOK URL" block under the current-config section. Surfaces the routable URL (with this tenant's UUID baked in) + Copy button. Owner pastes into Brivo dashboard → Webhooks. |
| `BRIVO.md` | Documented both webhook URL options (single-tenant env-var path + per-tenant `?tenant=` path). |

### Doug to do

`bash admin/deploy-functions.sh` — picks up brivo-webhook changes. No other action required; backward-compatible.

### What's now genuinely complete in Brivo Phase 1

Every Brivo Edge Function (6 of them + the shared helper) is multi-tenant aware. Per-tenant credential storage, per-tenant lockdown, per-tenant event passes, per-tenant hours sync, per-tenant webhook routing. 2nd Nature's env-var install keeps working unchanged. A second skatepark can be onboarded entirely through the Settings UI now.

### Genuinely-left Phase 2 items

- ~~Per-tenant drift check in brivo-sync-all full mode~~ — **DONE this session.** Drift check now iterates env-var-fallback account AND every `tenant_brivo_config` row with per-tenant credentials. Each orphan is tagged with `tenant_id` + `tenant_source` (env_vars / tenant_table) so the admin reconcile-report can attribute correctly.
- ~~Onboarding wizard for new parks~~ — **DONE this session (lightweight version).** Setup Status card on Dashboard refactored into a real onboarding wizard: setup readiness progress bar (% + green/total count), color-coded per-item rows, right-aligned "Configure →" action buttons that jump to the right Settings tab (or to migration-bundle SQL editor URL for db migrations). Replaces what would have been a separate wizard page with sharper actions on the existing surface. Heavier "first-run multi-step wizard" still possible Phase 3 if Doug wants a guided experience for non-technical owners.
- ~~Vision events CSV export~~ — **DONE this session.** "Events CSV" button on Settings → skateOS Vision Box card. Exports last 1000 events with joined camera + customer + Brivo cross-ref flag. Self-contained spreadsheet rows.

## Session log — 2026-05-15 actually-last-call (Per-tenant Brivo Phase 1 closeout)

Doug said "go" again. Finished what Phase 1 started: every Brivo Edge Function now resolves credentials per-tenant.

| Function | What changed |
|---|---|
| `_brivo/api.ts` | Added `extractJwt(req)` helper + documented `OwnerVerification` interface for the JWT-resolution pattern used across admin-triggered Edge Functions. |
| `brivo-sync-all` | Relaxed the env-var gate — per-customer credential resolution (via brivo-sync-customer) handles authentication. Drift check still env-var-based (Phase 2 will iterate per-tenant). |
| `brivo-issue-event-pass` | Now calls `loadBrivoEnvForTenant(sb, customer.tenant_id)` instead of `loadBrivoEnv()`. The synchronous-sync-when-in-window gate respects per-tenant credentials. |
| `brivo-sync-schedule` | Reads JWT → resolves `current_tenant_id` → loads per-tenant credentials. Uses `env.operatingHoursScheduleId` from the resolved env (not direct `Deno.env.get`). Error hints adapt based on credential source (table vs env). |
| `brivo-lockdown` | Major refactor — JWT-based tenant resolution + **tenant-scoped DB updates** (critical: previously would have suspended customers across all tenants in a multi-tenant install). The lockdown state in `app_settings` is also tenant-scoped now (uses `(tenant_id, key)` composite UNIQUE INDEX for upsert). |
| `brivo-webhook` | Signature verification now has a 2-step resolution: (1) try `BRIVO_WEBHOOK_SECRET` env var, (2) if that fails, parse body for brivo_user_id → look up customer → load that tenant's `webhook_secret` → try that. Backward-compat: pure env-var installs keep working. Multi-tenant installs route signature verification to the right park automatically. |

### What this means for white-label

**Every Brivo Edge Function is now multi-tenant aware** while remaining 100% backward-compatible with 2nd Nature's current env-var install. A second skatepark can sign up + paste their credentials via Settings → Brivo per-tenant credentials, and:
- Their members provision against THEIR Brivo account
- Their lockdown affects only THEIR active-members group
- Their door events route to THEIR webhook secret for verification
- Their hours sync to THEIR Brivo schedule
- Their event passes provision into THEIR active-members group

### What's left for Phase 2

- **Per-tenant webhook URLs** (`/brivo-webhook/<tenant_id>`) — would let signature verification skip the dual-attempt fallback, and unblock receiving events for unknown brivo_user_ids per tenant
- **Per-tenant drift check** in brivo-sync-all full mode — iterate each `tenant_brivo_config` row, list each park's group, find orphans per-tenant
- **Migration helper**: one-time script to copy 2nd Nature's env-var values into a `tenant_brivo_config` row for consistency (cosmetic — env fallback works fine indefinitely)

### Doug to do

`bash admin/deploy-functions.sh` — picks up changes to all 5 Brivo Edge Functions

---

## Session log — 2026-05-15 last-call (Per-tenant Brivo Phase 1)

White-label unlock. Doug said "go" — picked the biggest remaining unblocked item.

| Surface | Deliverable |
|---|---|
| Migration `069_tenant_brivo_config.sql` | New `tenant_brivo_config` table (one row per tenant) storing all Brivo credentials + config IDs. **Strict RLS — no SELECT/INSERT/UPDATE for any client role** (no policy defined = no access). Only `service_role` reads raw secrets via Edge Functions. Owner reads metadata via `brivo_config_status_for_current_tenant()` SECURITY DEFINER function which returns *_set booleans + last-4 hints, never raw secrets. Backward-compatible: 2nd Nature's current env-var setup keeps working unchanged. |
| `_brivo/api.ts` | New `loadBrivoEnvForTenant(sb, tenant_id)` async function. Resolution order: tenant_brivo_config row → BRIVO_* env vars → null. BrivoEnv interface extended with all per-tenant config fields (group IDs, AP IDs, schedule ID, webhook secret, auto_checkin flag, source: 'tenant_table' \| 'env_vars'). |
| Edge Function `brivo-save-config` | Owner-only credential management. Actions: save (partial-update — empty fields preserved), test (OAuth + API smoke test, stamps `last_verified_at`), delete (drops row → falls back to env vars). Verifies caller is owner via JWT + `is_owner()` RPC. Audit-logs all actions to webhook_log without echoing secrets. |
| Modified `brivo-sync-customer` | Credential resolution moved AFTER customer load so the customer's `tenant_id` drives the lookup. Falls back to env vars transparently. Group ID + AP IDs now come from `env.activeMembersGroupId` etc. (not direct Deno.env reads). |
| Settings UI | New "Brivo per-tenant credentials" card (owner-only, between main Brivo card + welcome email card). Status block shows ✓ / — per field with last-4 hints for client_id + api_key. Action row: Update credentials (modal with 9 fields), Test credentials, Delete (fall back to env vars). Modal is write-only — existing secrets are never read back; empty inputs preserve existing values. |
| Setup Status | Probe for mig 069. Header bumped to `006-069`. |
| Deploy script | `brivo-save-config` added to deploy-functions.sh |

### What this unlocks

A second skatepark can now sign up for skateOS without us reusing 2nd Nature's Brivo account. Each tenant has their own row in `tenant_brivo_config` + connects to their own Brivo dashboard. Edge Functions resolve credentials by tenant_id at request time.

### What's still pending for full multi-tenant Brivo

- Other Brivo Edge Functions (brivo-sync-all, brivo-webhook, brivo-issue-event-pass, brivo-lockdown, brivo-sync-schedule) still read env vars only. For now they'll work for 2nd Nature (env vars set) but won't pick up per-tenant configs. Same `loadBrivoEnvForTenant` swap needed in each — straightforward but multi-file. **brivo-sync-customer is the most-called function and IS now tenant-aware**, so 80% of the value is shipped.
- Per-tenant webhook URLs (so Brivo posts route to the right tenant without customer lookup) — currently relies on brivo_user_id → customer → tenant_id resolution which works for access events but not door-forced / intercom events when customer_id is null.

### Doug to do

1. **Apply migration 069** in Supabase SQL editor
2. **Redeploy Edge Functions**: `bash admin/deploy-functions.sh` — picks up `brivo-save-config` + the modified `brivo-sync-customer`
3. **Test the flow** (optional, only meaningful when you onboard a second park): Settings → Integrations → Brivo per-tenant credentials → Update credentials → save → Test credentials → verify ✓

Requires `BRIVO_OPERATING_HOURS_SCHEDULE_ID` secret. Returns dry-run preview when `dry_run=true`. Audit-logs every fire to webhook_log. Defensive against Brivo API shape variance — failure surfaces the raw response so owner can adjust the function. |

## Session log — 2026-05-15 late-late evening (Event passes)

Doug asked "what else?" — kept going.

| Surface | Deliverable |
|---|---|
| Migration `067_brivo_event_passes.sql` | New `brivo_event_passes` table (customer_id, valid_from, valid_until, status, reason, party_form_submission_id, issued_by). Multi-tenant RLS. Extends `brivo_member_desired` view: customers get access EITHER from active monthly/annual sub OR from an active event pass. New `desired_reason='event_pass'` value distinguishes the path. New `brivo_sweep_expired_event_passes()` RPC + pg_cron job `brivo-event-pass-sweep` running every 5 min — flips status='expired' on lapsed passes + flags customers for re-sync. |
| Edge Function `brivo-issue-event-pass` | POST {customer_id, valid_from, valid_until, reason, party_form_submission_id?, send_invite?}. Validates window (must be in future, max 30 days). Refuses to issue for banned customers. Warns when waiver is missing or expires before pass window. Inserts the pass + flags for sync; fires synchronous `brivo-sync-customer` call when window is live so customer can use door immediately. Audit-logs to webhook_log. |
| Admin UI | Customer detail Brivo panel gets a 4th action button "🎟️ Issue event pass" (owner-only, purple-outlined). Opens a modal with datetime-local pickers (defaults to next Saturday 2pm-6pm), reason field, send-invite checkbox. After issue, panel reloads and shows new "Event passes (N)" section — 🟢 LIVE NOW (green) / ⏰ SCHEDULED (blue) cards with Revoke buttons + collapsible past-passes block. |
| Setup Status | Probe for migration 067 — checks brivo_event_passes table presence. Header bumped to `006-067`. |

## Session log — 2026-05-15 evening (Brivo polish: lockdown + welcome editor)

Continued the momentum after the main door integration shipped. Added the highest-impact safety + customization features.

### What landed

| Surface | Deliverable |
|---|---|
| Edge Function | New `brivo-lockdown/index.ts` — engage/release actions. Engage lists all members in active-members group, parallel-revokes (concurrency 10), stamps `customers.brivo_credential_state='suspended'`, persists `app_settings.value.integrations.brivo.lockdown = {active, reason, set_at, set_by_email, removed, failed}`. Release flips flag off + re-flags every customer for normal 5-min cron re-evaluation. Audit-stamps both actions into `webhook_log` with source='brivo-lockdown'. |
| brivo-sync-customer | New lockdown gate at top of handler: when `lockdown.active === true`, refuses provision (forces customers into `suspended` state with sync_error stamp). Prevents the 5-min cron from undoing lockdown. |
| brivo-sync-customer welcome | Welcome email now reads custom subject + body from `app_settings.value.integrations.brivo.welcomeSubject` / `welcomeBody`. Empty strings fall back to the baked-in rich default. Custom bodies wrap inside the rose gradient header for branding consistency. Defensive sanitization strips `<script>` + `on*=` attributes. Variable interpolation: `{{first}}` / `{{biz}}` / `{{biz_phone}}` / `{{biz_address}}`. |
| Settings → Brivo | New "Brivo emergency lockdown" card (owner-only, only when Brivo enabled). Renders LOCKDOWN ACTIVE pill + reason callout + revoke count when active, or big red ENGAGE LOCKDOWN button when inactive. Engage requires reason + typed "LOCKDOWN" confirmation. New "Brivo welcome email" card with subject + body textareas + variable reference. New "Open Brivo dashboard →" link in the main Brivo card footer. |
| Sticky banner | New `_renderBrivoLockdownBanner()` function — wired into renderPage() cascade. Pulsing red banner across every admin page when lockdown is active: 🚨 BRIVO LOCKDOWN · reason · removed count · engaged-at timestamp · owner-only End-lockdown button. |
| Deploy | `admin/deploy-functions.sh` extended with `brivo-lockdown` deploy. |

- **Audit cache bug fix — DONE (2026-05-02).** The recently-deleted recovery card and the audit log card both wrote to `window._auditRowsCache`, racing — whichever rendered last won, so clicking an audit row could open the wrong snapshot. Fix: `openAuditDiff(idx, cacheKey)` now takes an explicit cache name; recovery rows pass `'_recoveryRowsCache'` so they read from their own array.
- **Mid-shift role switch — DONE (2026-05-02).** Same employee does multiple jobs in one shift (front desk + instructor mid-day). Schema (migration 008) already supported it via `time_entries.shift_type`; UI was missing the explicit switch. Personal clock-in widget on Timesheets now: (a) shows current role as a colored badge ("INSTRUCTOR" purple), (b) when clocked in, exposes a "Switch role to…" dropdown + Switch button that atomically clocks out the current entry and clocks back in under the new shift_type, with notes stamped on both. Two adjacent entries with different shift_types — accurate per-role hours / pay calculations downstream.
- **Lesson modal: customer-context hint — DONE (2026-05-02).** When the cashier picks a skater in the New Lesson modal, an inline hint line shows: red "3/4 no-shows in 60d — consider deposit" if chronic, amber "1 no-show in 60d", waiver-state pill (red if missing/expired), active membership ("10-Pack Punch Card (3/10 left)"), loyalty point balance. Surfaces the same context as customer-detail without forcing the cashier to bounce out of the booking flow. Pre-fires on modal open so deeplink customers also see it. Pure JS, no extra DB calls (reads loaded customers/lessons/subscriptions arrays).
- **Customer detail "Schedule lesson" remembers their usual instructor — DONE (2026-05-02).** The Schedule lesson deeplink on customer detail now scans the customer's lesson history (sorted desc by scheduled_at), finds their most-recently-used instructor, and pre-fills it on the new lesson modal. Plus the existing customer pre-fill. Saves the cashier from re-picking the regular instructor for repeat skaters. The instructor availability hint also fires immediately so they see the green "on shift now" pill or "on staff" hint without typing.
- **Lesson modal: time-conflict warning — DONE (2026-05-02).** `saveLesson` now checks for overlapping lessons on the same instructor before persisting. If found, surfaces a confirm dialog: "WARNING — Doug is already booked Sat 4p for Tommy (60min). Schedule anyway?" Skips the check when no instructor is named (open booking) and excludes cancelled/no-show lessons from the conflict pool. Edit mode excludes the current lesson's own row. Cashier can override and proceed (sometimes back-to-back overlaps are intentional — e.g., overlapping camp + private). Pure JS.
- **Lesson modal: type-aware default duration + capacity — DONE (2026-05-02).** On NEW lessons, picking a lesson type from the dropdown auto-bumps the duration field (private 60 / group 90 / camp 180 / event 120 / birthday 120) AND nudges capacity up if low (camp → at least 8, group → at least 4). On edit, leaves the saved duration alone (no clobber). Cashier can override either. Saves the "set type, then re-type duration to match" cycle.
- **Lesson modal: "Save & schedule another" — DONE (2026-05-02).** New outline button in the lesson modal footer (only on create, not edit). Saves the current lesson and immediately re-opens a fresh modal with date/time/instructor/type/duration/price/capacity all pre-filled from the just-saved entry — only the customer field is blanked + auto-focused. Designed for camp signups where a parent registers 8 kids back-to-back, or quick lesson booking runs at a single time slot. Toast says "Saved · ready for next attendee".
- **Lesson modal: instructor availability hint — DONE (2026-05-02).** `_uniqueInstructors()` now merges historical lesson instructors with active staff (role 'instructor' or 'owner') so brand-new instructors appear before they've taught. `_clockedInInstructorNames()` returns the right-now set. As you type in the lesson modal's Instructor input, an inline hint shows: green pulsing dot + "On shift now" if clocked in as instructor, gray "On staff" if known but not clocked in, or amber "New instructor — will appear in future lessons" if neither. Datalist also gets `label="on shift now"` for browsers that surface it. Pure JS.
- **Resource view: shift-overlay shading — DONE (2026-05-02).** Builds on the Lessons "Staff" view: cells where the column's instructor is NOT clocked in as `instructor` for the current day get a subtle diagonal-stripe gray background. Tooltip explains "outside their instructor shift today — booking allowed but verify". Cells stay clickable (some bookings legitimately need to be made before/after a shift). Instructors with no instructor shift today get no shading at all (unknown availability ≠ unavailable). Reads `time_entries` for the day, treating still-clocked-in entries as covering the rest of the operating window.
- **Configurable calendar hours — DONE (2026-05-02).** New "Calendar hours" pair on Settings → Operations: Day starts at (5am–noon) + Day ends at (5pm–11pm), defaults 9am–9pm. Both the new Lessons "Staff" view + the Reports "Sales by hour" heatmap now read from `settings.operations.calDayStart` / `calDayEnd` instead of hardcoded values. Auto-floors end > start with a 4h minimum so the grid never collapses. Pure JS.
- **Lessons "Staff" resource-scheduling view — DONE (2026-05-02).** New view toggle on Lessons page alongside Week / Day. Industry-standard scheduling-software pattern (Google Calendar / Calendly / Acuity / clinic EMR layout): instructors as columns, time-of-day (9am–9pm) as rows, color-coded blocks per lesson. Empty cells are clickable — pre-fills the lesson modal with that instructor + that hour, so scheduling is one click away. Currently-clocked-in instructors (open `time_entries` with `shift_type='instructor'`) get a green pulsing-dot badge on their column header. Group lessons show a "3/8" capacity pill inside the block. Click any block → opens the existing edit modal. Pure JS — no schema change.
- **Auto-SMS receipts toggle — DONE (2026-05-02).** New `settings.autoSmsReceipts` (default OFF since Twilio costs money) on Settings → Business. When enabled AND Twilio is on AND customer has a phone but no email (or email auto-send is off), `smsReceipt(true)` fires 600ms after the receipt modal paints. Idempotent — won't double-send on re-render. Avoids double-pinging customers who already get the email receipt. Falls back silently to console.warn on failure (no toast spam during quiet auto-fire).
- **Customer detail: "last visit" relative time — DONE (2026-05-02).** Customer-since line now also shows `last visit Xm/h/d/w/mo ago`, color-coded green (recent), amber (>30d dormant), red (>90d lapsed). Reads from `c.last_visit_at` first, falls back to newest sale's created_at. At-a-glance recency check during phone calls.
- **Sales History quick-range chips — DONE (2026-05-02).** Strip of one-click chips above the search bar: Today / Yesterday / This week (Monday-start) / Last week / This month / Last month / Clear. Each populates the from/to date pickers and re-runs `filterHistory()`. Saves the date-picker fiddling for the most-common reconciliation slices. Pure JS.
- **Audit log CSV export — DONE (2026-05-02).** New CSV button on the Admin actions audit log card. Honors all current filters (table / actor / action / from / to). Pulls up to 1000 rows for export so multi-month windows fit. Columns: when / actor / action / table / row_id / changed fields list / old JSON (truncated 500c) / new JSON (truncated 500c). Use cases: "who edited this customer's loyalty?" forensics, GDPR data-access requests, year-end change-control reviews.
- **Webhook log CSV export — DONE (2026-05-02).** Owner-only CSV button on the Webhook log card (Activity Log page). Pulls last 500 events (vs 50 on-screen) so audit exports cover a real time window. Columns: when / source / event_type / event_id / status / linked table+id / error / payload (JSON-stringified, truncated 500 chars). Use cases: chargeback dispute support ("show me every Helcim event for this card"), Smartwaiver compliance audit, post-mortem on a failed webhook delivery.
- **Equipment CSV export — DONE (2026-05-02).** New CSV button on Loaners page header (between status filter and Add gear). Sorted by asset_tag. Per-row columns include any current open loan (customer name resolved from `customers`, checkout time, due_at, loan notes) so the export is self-contained — no need to cross-reference equipment_loans separately. Use cases: insurance asset list, year-end inventory audit, lost-gear write-offs.

Day-of-week × hour grid (9am–9pm operational window), color-graded by gross revenue. Peak callout: "Saturday 4p ($2,140 over 90d)". Hover any cell for "Sat 4p: $2,140" tooltip. Pure JS, uses already-loaded validSales array — no extra DB roundtrip. Drives staffing decisions: which Saturday afternoons need a second cashier? When can the morning shift be cut?

- **Lessons CSV export — DONE (2026-05-02).** New CSV button in the Lessons page header. Honors all current filters (range + instructor + type + status from the filter shipped earlier today). Columns: scheduled_at, skater, instructor, type, capacity, booked count, duration, price, status, attended_at, reminder_sent_at, notes. Footer row totals `earned` from completed lessons only — drop-in payroll: filter to "completed for Doug last month" + click CSV → file has the answer at the bottom. Toast confirms count + total. Pure JS.
- **Activity Log (inventory) date + direction filters — DONE (2026-05-02).** Activity Log search bar gains from-date, to-date, and direction (Stock IN / Stock OUT) dropdowns alongside the existing text search and CSV button. - **Loyalty CSV export — DONE (2026-05-02).** New CSV button on the Loyalty page's "Top members" card header. - **Sale detail modal: cashier + tip recipient cells — DONE (2026-05-02).** Sale detail modal now shows the Cashier (resolved from `actor_id` via staffList) and, when tip > 0, the Tip recipient (resolved from `tip_for_staff_id`, green) right next to Customer + Payment + Mobile run. Useful for tip-pool dispute resolution and "who rang this comp?" investigations. Pure JS — schema's already there.
- **Cross-page POS cart pill — DONE (2026-05-02).** New top-bar button "🛒 Cart: 3 items" appears whenever `cart` has items AND the current page isn't POS. Clicking it jumps back to POS to resume the in-progress sale. Hidden on POS itself (the cart's already visible) and hidden when cart is empty. Refreshed on every cart mutation (`renderCart` hook) and on every page navigation (`go()` hook). Closes the "I added items, walked over to check on a customer, forgot what I was ringing up" gap.
- **Customer merge — DONE (2026-05-02).** Migration `037_customer_merge.sql` adds `merge_customers(p_keep_id, p_drop_id, p_reason)` RPC. Owner-only (is_owner check inside). Moves FK customer_id across 10 tables (sales, lessons, subscriptions, loyalty_transactions, checkins, incidents, lesson_attendees with UNIQUE-conflict pre-cleanup, invoices, orders, equipment_loans), each block guarded by EXCEPTION undefined_table so it works even when newer migrations aren't applied. Sums loyalty cached balance. Stamps `[Merged customer NAME (uuid) on DATE: REASON]` into the kept row's notes. Deletes the dropped row. Returns JSON with per-table moved counts. Dupe finder UI now shows the most-active row first (auto-suggested KEEP) and "→ Merge into top" buttons next to each other row. Confirms with explicit "PERMANENTLY DELETED" wording. **Migration must still be applied.**
- **Customer duplicate finder — DONE (2026-05-02).** New owner-only "Find dupes (N)" button on Customers page (only shows when N > 0, amber styling). Click opens a modal that clusters customers sharing a normalized email or digits-only phone (10+ digits, so partial matches don't false-positive). Each cluster shows row name + email + phone + visits + spend, with an "Open" button to jump to that customer's detail. Detection-only for now — merging requires moving FKs across sales / subs / lessons / loyalty / etc, which is a future migration. For now Doug can compare side-by-side and manually copy notes / delete the dup. Useful at scale: skaters create duplicate records from typos, parents register kids twice, etc.
- **Auto-expire past-due memberships button — DONE (2026-05-02).** New red dashboard alert chip "N memberships past end_date — flip to expired" appears when any active subscription's `end_date < now()`. Click → `autoExpirePastDue()` confirms then batch-PATCHes each row to status='expired' with an audit stamp `[Auto-expired DATE by NAME — past end_date]`. Pure JS, no migration — until Doug ships a server cron equivalent (similar to migration 030's auto_resume), this keeps the active-members count accurate. Tolerant of partial failures.
- **Receipt SMS via Twilio — DONE (2026-05-02).** Receipt modal now offers a "Text receipt" button when the customer has a phone on file. Twilio-on path fires through `send-sms` Edge Function with body "skateOS — Receipt #1234: $25.00 (saved $5). Thanks for skating!". Twilio-off path falls back to a `sms:` link that opens the device SMS app (works on iPad). E.164 normalization (defaults +1 prefix). Handles the "customer paid cash, no email, wants the receipt texted" workflow without hand-typing into the staff phone.

- **Receipt "you saved $X today" line — DONE (2026-05-02).** Whenever a sale's discount ≥ $1 (sums promo + loyalty redemption + industry-tag auto-discount), all three receipt formats — in-app modal, emailed HTML receipt, thermal-printer popup — show a green "★ You saved $X today" line below the total. Reinforces value to the customer (especially loyalty/promo users) without changing the math. Pure JS.
- **Sales CSV export — staff & tip-recipient columns — DONE (2026-05-02).** `exportSalesCSV` now includes Cashier (resolved from `actor_id` via staffList lookup), Tip recipient (resolved from `tip_for_staff_id`), and Refunded (the partial-refund amount from migration 034). - **Daily digest tip-pool snapshot — DONE (2026-05-02).** Existing `daily-digest` Edge Function now also queries `actor_id` + `tip_for_staff_id` from yesterday's sales, builds `tipsByStaff[recipient_id] = sum(tip)` (falling back to actor_id when tip_for_staff_id is null), looks up display names from `staff` table for any matched ids, and inserts a "Tip pool — yesterday" section into the email after the main stats. Each row shows name + amount, ranked by amount desc. Section auto-hides when no tips were collected. JSON response gains `summary.yesterday.tip_pool: [{id, name, amount}]` for downstream automation. Re-deploy via `bash admin/deploy-functions.sh`.
- **Sales-by-staff: tip recipient column — DONE (2026-05-02).** Reports → Sales by staff card now shows two tip columns: "Tips at till" (tips on sales the staff member rang) and "Tips received" (tips assigned to them via `tip_for_staff_id`). Falls back to "tips at till = tips received" when `tip_for_staff_id` is null on a sale (covers all pre-shipping rows). Instructors who don't ring sales but receive lesson tips appear as a "tips only" row at the bottom of the table — sales/gross/avg shown as `—` so they don't pollute the ranking but their tip earnings stay visible. - **Auto-checkout lingering sessions cron — DONE (2026-05-02).** Migration `036_auto_checkout_cron.sql` adds a `notes` column to `checkins` (so the audit stamp has somewhere to live) + an `auto_checkout_lingering(p_threshold_min INT DEFAULT 480)` RPC + a daily pg_cron at 08:00 UTC (~3am ET, well past every park's close). The RPC closes any `checkins` row that's been open longer than the threshold (default 8h, hard-floored at 30 min) and stamps `[Auto-closed at park-close cron — was open N min]` into the row's notes. Safety net for when staff forgets to hit "End session" — the mass-close button shipped earlier handles the proactive case; this catches the slip-throughs. **Migration must still be applied.**
- **Email opt-out — full coverage of admin send paths — DONE (2026-05-02).** Two more gates added on top of the staff toggle + segment filter: (1) `_ciRenewEmail` (punch-card renewal nudge from check-in) now refuses to send when `c.email_opt_out_at` is set — toasts "X has opted out — try SMS or in-person" — and the email body itself gains the standard unsubscribe footer. (2) Marketing campaign send (`sendCampaign`) appends an unsubscribe link footer to every email body with the per-recipient customer-id URL. Receipts and other transactional emails (waiver helper, invoice send) intentionally skip the gate — CAN-SPAM exempts transactional/relationship messages. Both helpers compute the unsubscribe URL from `APP_CONFIG.appBaseUrl` (falls back to current page origin).
- **Email opt-out — staff toggle + marketing-segment honoring — DONE (2026-05-02).** Two follow-ups to the 035 base: (1) Customer detail modal now shows a 🔕 button next to email when not opted-out (mark them out — used when they ask in person) and an undo arrow when opted-out (re-subscribe with documented consent). Email displays struck-through with a red "opted out 2026-05-02" chip when set. Both toggle paths call the migration 035 RPCs (`email_opt_out` for either staff or customer-facing, `email_opt_in` staff-only). (2) Marketing campaign builder's `_segmentRecipients` now filters out opted-out customers BEFORE applying segment criteria — opt-outs are absolute, no segment can override. Pure JS, no schema change.
- **Email opt-out / CAN-SPAM compliance — DONE (2026-05-02).** Migration `035_email_opt_out.sql` adds `customers.email_opt_out_at TIMESTAMPTZ` + a public `email_opt_out(p_customer_id UUID)` RPC (anon-callable, SECURITY DEFINER, idempotent — returns success even if UUID maps to nothing to prevent enum attacks) + a staff-only `email_opt_in(...)` for manual reversal. New static page `admin/unsubscribe.html` reads `?cid=<uuid>` from URL, validates UUID format, calls the RPC, shows confirmation. `send-lesson-reminders` Edge Function now selects `customers.email_opt_out_at` and skips opted-out rows; lesson reminder email gets a small `<hr>` + "Don't want lesson reminders? Unsubscribe." footer with the customer-specific URL. `birthday-greetings` Edge Function does the same — filters out opted-out customers at the query level + adds the unsubscribe footer. `APP_BASE_URL` env var (defaults to `https://app.skateos.com`) controls the unsubscribe link domain. **Migration must still be applied + Edge Functions re-deployed.**
- **POS today's running total strip — DONE (2026-05-02).** Above the cart on POS, a small green strip shows "Today: $342.50 · 8 sales" — at-a-glance running total for the cashier across all of today's completed sales (refunded_amount subtracted, voided/refunded status excluded). - **POS: cart memo field — DONE (2026-05-09).** Short text input above the held/parked sales row on POS — owner-tunable fulfillment context that surfaces on the receipt + sale detail. **Use cases**: "for Tommy's birthday" / "rush ship NY" / "leave at front desk for pickup" / "gift wrap pink" / "subscriber discount applied verbally" / "first-time visit comp note". 120-char cap, `[ ]` chars stripped to avoid colliding with the audit-stamp regex pattern. **Stamps to `sales.notes`** as `[Memo: text]` alongside other audit markers (Tax exempt / Comped / Loyalty redeemed / Promo code / Industry discount). **Receipt rendering** (in-app modal AND emailed HTML) extracts the memo via regex + surfaces in italic between the customer line and the footer with a 📝 emoji prefix. - **POS: daily revenue goal meter — DONE (2026-05-09).** Pairs with the weekly goal tracker (Reports card) by adding the daily-level focus pinned at top of POS. New Settings field "Daily revenue goal ($)" in Settings → Business — defaults to 0 (disabled), or auto-derives from `weeklyRevenueGoal / 7` when left blank but weekly is set. **POS top strip** (above the today running total) renders only when goal > 0: white card with header line "🎯 Daily goal · $500 · 68%" + progress bar (8px tall) + "$160 to go" sub-line OR "🎉 Goal hit · $42 over" when at 100%+. **Color-graded progress bar**: red <50% / amber 50-74% / green 75-99% / green ≥100%. **Park-wide totals** (not per-cashier) — the goal is the shop's number, while the existing "My today" filter handles per-cashier tracking. Pure JS, no migration. Drives intra-day focus + accountability — cashier sees the gap closing in real time.

- **Customer detail: comprehensive health score — DONE (2026-05-09).** Owner-only consolidated view of customer health. **Single A-F grade** with breakdown panel that aggregates 5 components scored 0-20 each (totaling /100). **Components**: (1) **Visit cadence** — days since last visit vs personal avg gap (recent = high score, stale = low). (2) **Reliability** — completed / (completed + cancelled + no-show) over last 60 days of lessons. (3) **Loyalty engagement** — tier index + recent loyalty-transaction activity (+4 boost when active in last 30 days). (4) **Spend trajectory** — last 90d revenue vs prior 90d (refund-net). (5) **Tenure** — relationship length, with penalty halving the tenure score when last-visit is >90d stale. **Grade map**: A ≥90 / B ≥80 / C ≥70 / D ≥60 / F <60. **Layout**: big A-F letter (3rem, color-graded green to red) + 1-line narrative ("Outstanding — recent, reliable, growing, engaged. Lock in for the long haul." / "At risk — multiple weak components. Worth a personal touch.") + auto-detected weakest component when grade is below B ("⚠ Weakest: Reliability (6/20) — 4/8 lessons completed in 60d"). Below the headline: 5 progress bars one per component, each with score + 1-line detail. Footer disclaimer documents the heuristic + thresholds. Skips render when customer is too new for a meaningful score (visits<2 + spend<$10). Pure JS using already-loaded customers/sales/lessons/loyalty arrays. Useful for retention conversations + at-risk customer identification + power-user identification (A-grades). Drives focused effort: instead of "should I message Tommy?", owner sees "Tommy is C — weakest is cadence — reach out about a comeback offer."

"× Remove" per row with confirm. **Defaults seeded** when no tiers configured: Bronze ($0) "Welcome — every visit earns points · Member-only birthday comp", Silver ($250) "5% off retail · Priority booking on weekends · Free wax with deck purchase", Gold ($1000) "10% off retail · Priority booking on all sessions · Free session every 5 referrals · Front-of-line on busy days". **Persistence**: writes to `app_settings.value.loyalty.tiers` JSONB (key='all'). Tolerant of missing migration 004 — falls back to localStorage. **Customer detail surface**: tier-colored panel below the loyalty actions row showing customer's CURRENT tier perks as a bulleted list + progress bar to next tier with $X away + collapsible "What unlocks at [Next tier]?" preview. Auto-hides when no tiers have perks defined (clean for fresh installs that haven't configured). Drives retention motivation — customer sees "I'm $87 from Gold — 10% off retail kicks in" instead of just an abstract badge. Pure JS, no migration. me.html portal display of perks is a nice-to-have follow-up not blocking this ship.
- **Reports: incidents by park area heatmap — DONE (2026-05-09).** Owner-only Reports card. Async-fetches last 90 days of `incidents` rows (mig 010) + buckets by `park_area`. Surfaces high-risk zones for safety reviews + insurance conversations. **3-up headline strip**: Total incidents / Serious incidents (ER + EMS) — red when >0, green when 0 / Areas with incidents. **Per-area heatmap rows**: bar width proportional to incident count, **bar color graded by average severity** (red ≥urgent_care+, orange ≥first_aid+, amber ≥first_aid, green ≥none) so the visual instantly differentiates "lots of minor stuff in the lobby" from "few but serious in the bowl". Per-row severity breakdown line ("3 EMS · 2 ER · 5 urgent · 7 first aid") + top-3 incident types ("Top: collision (5), fall (3), head impact (2)"). Pretty-prints area names (street → "Street", snake_run → "Snake Run"). **Auto-callouts**: 🚨 "Hotspot: [Area] drives 40%+ of incidents — walk it: pad placement, sightlines, signage, supervised hours" / red "X serious incidents (ER + EMS) — cross-ref Incidents page filter + open corrective-action queue + insurer should see these proactively" / green "Zero serious incidents — healthy state, mention in marketing + insurance renewal". Footer link jumps to Incidents page for drill-down. Tolerant of missing migration 010 (silent no-render). Pure JS, no migration. Closes the "where do incidents cluster?" gap that the per-incident list view couldn't answer at-a-glance.
- **Reports: subscription churn rate trend — DONE (2026-05-09).** Pairs with the existing MRR/ARR card by adding the trend lens — MRR shows current state, this shows whether the membership base is healthy or leaking. **12-week rolling chart**: per-week churn % = (cancelled + expired with end_date in week) / (active at start of week). Active-at-start computed from start_date ≤ weekStart AND (end_date IS NULL OR end_date > weekStart). Day-passes + comped subs excluded. **Headline strip**: Last 4 weeks rate (color-coded — green <4% / amber 4-8% / red ≥8%) + trend chip (red ↑ when up ≥0.5pt, green ↓ when down) + raw 12-week count "8 churned · 14 new". **Bar chart**: 12 weekly bars + current partial week dimmed. **Industry-benchmarked auto-callouts**: 🚨 "Weekly churn ≥8% — leaking bucket. Even strong acquisition can't outrun this. Investigate end-of-cycle without renewal? Quality issue? Send 'what made you leave' survey" / amber "Elevated churn. Industry-typical for recreation membership is 1-3%/week" / ✓ "Healthy — you're inside the 1-3% recreation benchmark" / red "Trend up X pts vs prior 4 wks — catch this early before it compounds" / green "Trend down — keep doing what you changed" / ✓ "Net positive growth — N new vs M churned" / 🚨 "Net negative — base is shrinking. Acquisition needs a push or churn needs a fix (probably both)". 12-week window long enough to catch real trends. Pure JS, uses already-loaded subscriptions array. Lives between MRR card and payment-methods card on Reports.
- **Mobile bus end-of-run cash reconciliation — DONE (2026-05-09).** Real ops feature paralleling the daily-reconcile flow (mig 013) but at the mobile-run scale. The existing run-detail modal already had units variance (per-product physical count vs bus_inventory expected). Now adds the **cash variance lens**: payment-method breakdown of run sales (cash / card / gift card / other — split-payment-aware via `sales.payments` JSONB) + cash-counted input fields + live-update variance pill. **3-up cash inputs**: Cash float started + Cash counted at close + live "Net collected vs Expected" delta. **Color-coded variance pill**: green ✓ when |Δ| < $0.01, green "rounding" when ≤$1, amber "⚠ variance" when ≤$5, red "⚠⚠" when >$5. Detail line below: "Net cash collected: $147 · Expected from cash sales: $145" + red warning text on significant variance. **Close-out flow upgraded**: when variance is >$5 + owner clicks "Close out run", the confirm dialog escalates with the variance breakdown forcing acknowledgment ("Cash variance of $12 detected. Closing locks this run. Proceed anyway?"). On close, **audit-stamps the reconcile data** into `mobile_runs.notes`: `[Reconcile YYYY-MM-DD by ACTOR · cash start=$100 counted=$252 expected=$145 variance=+$7]` for full trail. Closed runs show the stamp inline (read-only) when re-opened. Toast confirms variance state. **Refunded_amount handled**: net gross (total - refunded) used everywhere instead of raw total. Pure JS, no migration. Closes the financial-trust gap for mobile shop runs — now Doug knows cash drawer balanced correctly OR knows the exact variance amount + when it happened.
- **Reports: lesson cancellation rate trend — DONE (2026-05-09).** Owner-only Reports card. Pairs with the existing "Lesson cancellation reasons" card by adding the trend lens — reasons answers WHY, this answers WHEN/IF. **12-week rolling chart**: Mon-Sun buckets ending with current partial week (dimmed at 50% opacity), color-graded green ≤15% / amber 15-25% / red ≥25%, height proportional to rate, rate % printed above each bar, hover tooltip "Sep 23: 4 cancelled of 18 scheduled (22.2%) · current/partial". **Headline strip**: Last 4 weeks rate (color-coded green/amber/red) + trend chip (red ↑ when up ≥1pt vs prior 4 weeks, green ↓ when down) + raw count "4 cancelled / 30 scheduled". **Cancel-event date detection**: parses `[Cancelled YYYY-MM-DD]` audit stamps so a lesson scheduled 90 days ago and cancelled today shows up in THIS WEEK's bucket (the operational signal we want — when did the cancel happen, not when was the original lesson). Falls back to scheduled_at when stamp missing. Block-time entries (`[BLOCK ...]` instructor lunch/training) excluded. **Auto-callouts**: red "Cancel rate ≥25% — high. Pairs poorly with growth: every cancel = lost revenue + instructor downtime" / amber "Cancel rate elevated, investigate dominant reason via the cancellation-reasons card below" / green "Cancel rate healthy" / red "Trend up X pts — investigate: instructor changes? weather? policy shift?" / green "Trend down X pts — whatever you changed, keep doing it". 12-week window long enough to catch real trends but short enough to be relevant. Pure JS, no migration. Lives between cancellation-reasons card and stockout card on Reports.

- **Customer detail + lesson modal: chronic-canceller flag — DONE (2026-05-09).** Parallels the existing chronic-no-show counter (3+ no-shows in 60 days) by adding cancellation tracking. They're communicating but it's a pattern — consider a non-refundable deposit or reduced last-minute flexibility." Falls back to scheduled_at when stamp is missing. 30-day window is tighter than the 60-day no-show window — recent cancel pattern is more actionable. Pure JS, no migration. Closes the operational gap that the no-show flag was missing — many parks have customers who DO call to cancel but do it constantly, and the front desk needs to surface that pattern to inform deposit policy decisions.
- **Loyalty: gift points to another customer — DONE (2026-05-09).** Owner-only feature for transferring loyalty points between customers. Use cases: parent → kid ("transfer my points to my son"), regulars gifting to friends, owner consolidating duplicate accounts after a merge that lost loyalty. New "🪁 Gift" button on customer detail loyalty actions row (only visible when customer has balance > 0 + viewer is owner). **Modal flow**: shows sender info card with current balance + recipient picker (excludes self, sorted by name + email-disambiguated), live-update preview as recipient is picked ("→ Tommy K currently has 50 pts"), points input with min/max bounds tied to sender's balance, live-update "after" preview ("After gift: Sarah 300 pts · Tommy 200 pts" or red ⚠ when exceeding balance), required reason field for audit. **Implementation pure JS, no migration**: writes two `loyalty_transactions` rows in sequence — sender row with `delta=-pts, reason='gift_sent', ref_type='gift_sent', ref_id=recipientId` then recipient row with `delta=+pts, reason='gift_received', ref_type='gift_received', ref_id=fromId`. Both fire the existing migration 006 `loyalty_apply_delta` trigger which updates `customers.loyalty_points` automatically. **Pair-linkage** via ref_type/ref_id so the audit log shows the matched pair. **Customer notes audit-stamped** on both sides ("[Gifted 100 pts to Tommy on 2026-05-09 by Doug: parent transfer]" + "[Received 100 pts from Sarah ...]") for human-readable forensics. **Partial-failure handling**: if sender debit succeeds but recipient credit fails, surfaces a clear toast pointing the owner toward Adjust to reverse — rather than silently leaving an orphan row. Confirm-dialog shows the full state diff before firing. Pairs naturally with the existing referral bonus + tier-progress + redemption flows. Closes the "I want my points to go to my kid's account" workflow that previously required adjusting two accounts manually with bookkeeping notes.

- **Affiliate program — phase 2: me.html portal dashboard — BUILT (2026-05-09).** Self-serve affiliate dashboard for enrolled team riders. Auto-shows on `me.html` (the customer self-serve portal) when the signed-in customer has an affiliate_codes row. **Section content**: rose-purple gradient card with "🏆 You're a team rider!" header, giant code box (white-on-rose-purple) with copy button + native-share + SMS + email share intents, 4-up stats (referrals / earned / driven / pending payout), public-profile URL link (opens in new tab), milestone-progress nudge ("🏆 2 more referrals until your next $25 bonus!" — auto-hides at exact milestone), collapsible recent-earnings list (last 10) with kind label + date + amount + status pill (PAID green / pending amber / reversed red). **Security fix in mig 045**: amended migration 045 with new SECURITY DEFINER RPC `my_affiliate_dashboard()` that resolves current customer via `current_customer_id()` (mig 019) and returns ONLY their own affiliate_codes row + program info + last 20 earnings. Closes a real PII leak — direct `affiliate_codes` / `affiliate_earnings` table reads in customer portal would have exposed every other customer's earnings (the staff-all RLS policy `USING (true)` includes the `authenticated` role, which covers customer-portal magic-link sessions). The RPC is rigidly scoped + GRANTed to `authenticated` so the same role can call it but only sees their own data. me.html now calls this RPC instead of querying tables directly. Tolerant of missing migration / missing RPC (silent fail, section stays hidden). Pure JS frontend, server-side privacy guarantee. - **Affiliate / team rider program — BUILT (2026-05-09).** Substantial white-label feature. Migration `045_affiliate_program.sql` adds 4 tables: **affiliate_programs** (one row per tenant, configurable reward kind = percent_commission / percent_first_only / flat_per_referral / points_per_dollar / + reward_value + attribution_window_days [default 90] + min_first_purchase + lifetime_cap + bonus_threshold_count + bonus_value_dollars for milestone rewards), **affiliate_codes** (one per enrolled customer, UNIQUE on code globally + UNIQUE on (program_id, customer_id), with bio/social_handles/photo_url for public profile + cached counters total_referrals/total_revenue/total_earned/total_paid for fast leaderboard), **affiliate_earnings** (append-only ledger with status workflow pending → approved → paid + paid_via/paid_reference for payouts + reversal kind for refunds), **affiliate_redemptions** (every code-use audit log). Plus `customers.affiliate_code_id` + `affiliate_attributed_at` columns so the buyer-attribution lookup is O(1). **Auto-earn trigger** (`affiliate_auto_earn`) fires on sales INSERT/UPDATE-of-status when buyer has affiliate_code_id set + within attribution window; computes earning per program kind; idempotent via UNIQUE INDEX on (sale_id, earning_kind); guards against self-purchase, lifetime cap, min-first-purchase threshold; refreshes denormalized counters; checks milestone bonus threshold and inserts bonus row when N-th referral milestone is hit. **Refund reversal trigger** (`affiliate_reverse_earnings`) mirrors mig 028's loyalty pattern — when sale flips completed → refunded/voided, inserts negative earning + flips original to status='reversed'. **Two RPCs**: `affiliate_code_lookup(p_code)` (anon-permissioned, returns minimal profile info for the public profile page) + `affiliate_attach_customer(p_customer_id, p_code, p_context, p_sale_id)` (locks attribution to first-code-used, records redemption regardless). RLS: programs+earnings+redemptions staff-only; codes anon-readable when enabled (powers the public profile). Default program seeded: 10% commission, 90-day window, $25 bonus every 5 referrals. **Admin UI**: new "Team Riders" link under Programs sidebar. Owner-only page with stats strip (active riders / lifetime referrals / driven revenue / total earned / owed-unpaid), program-summary card with one-click edit, leaderboard table (rank icon, code, referrals, driven revenue, earned, owed pill, status, click row to drill in), recent earnings table (last 30 with click-to-detail), enroll modal (customer picker excluding already-enrolled + auto-suggest code from first name + bio + IG/TikTok handles + internal notes + live public-URL preview), affiliate detail modal (photo + code + 4-up stats + share row + earnings table with per-row mark-paid button), program-config modal (4 reward kinds + window + min-first + lifetime cap + milestone bonus threshold), CSV export of all earnings. **POS wiring**: new "Team rider code" input below Gift card on POS form. `applyAffiliateCode` calls the RPC, validates code+enabled state, refuses self-referral + Walk-in carts, surfaces affiliate name + referral count inline, stashes `window._posAffiliateCode` for finalizeSale to commit via `_posCommitAffiliate(saleId, customerId)` post-completion (calls `affiliate_attach_customer` RPC; trigger handles the earning insert). `clearCart` resets affiliate state alongside other POS state. **Customer detail wiring**: `_renderCustomerAffiliatePanel(id)` async-fetches both this customer's own affiliate_codes row (when enrolled — renders rose-purple stats card with code + referrals/driven/earned/owed + Copy URL + Open profile + jump to Earnings page) AND the affiliate that referred THIS customer (when `affiliate_code_id` is set — renders "Referred by [Name] (code XXX) attributed YYYY-MM-DD" pill). Owner-only "Enroll as team rider" CTA button when not enrolled. Silent on missing migration. **Public affiliate profile page**: new `admin/affiliate.html?code=X` — clean rose-purple-themed standalone page (works on mobile + desktop, no admin auth needed). Loads via the anon `affiliate_code_lookup` RPC. Shows photo (or initials fallback) + name + biz-name role + bio + social handles + giant code box with copy + native-share + SMS + email share buttons + 2-up stats (referrals + driven revenue) + CTA back to home + map link. **Pure-JS share intent**: native `navigator.share` falls back to clipboard. Pre-built sharing message: "[Name] wants you to use their code XYZ at [Biz]!" Migration backlog now 006→045 (40 total). Public URL pattern: `https://app.skateos.com/affiliate.html?code=TOMMY10`. **Needs: apply migration 045.** Phase 2 follow-ups (next loop ticks): me.html portal affiliate dashboard for the rider's own self-serve view + payout-history CSV export per affiliate.
- **Reports: customer LTV distribution histogram — DONE (2026-05-09).** Owner-only Reports card paired with the existing top-customers leaderboard — leaderboard names individuals, this surfaces the population distribution. Pure JS using already-loaded `customers` array, no DB roundtrip. **Six skatepark-relevant brackets**: <$25 / $25–100 / $100–250 / $250–500 / $500–1000 / $1000+. **4-up headline strip**: customers-with-spend count + % of base / Avg LTV (green) / Median LTV (with "half spend more, half less" sub) / Lifetime revenue. **Histogram bars** color-graded gray → blue → green → amber → orange → pink as LTV rises, widths proportional to busiest bucket, count + % of base + revenue + % of revenue per row. **Pareto callout** computes what % of customers represent 80% of revenue — surfaces "the top 12 customers (8% of base) drive 80% of lifetime revenue" with classic-80/20 vs healthy-distribution vs distributed-widely narrative. **Pattern auto-callouts**: ⚠ "Long tail of low-spenders — 60%+ of customers spend under $100 lifetime, push 2nd-visit conversion or review onboarding flow" / 🏆 "5+ high-LTV customers ($1000+) — these deserve personalized thank-yous, comps, or merch" / ✓ "Strong middle — 40%+ of customers in $100–500 bracket means punch cards / lessons / monthly memberships are working." Methodology note clarifies bucketing uses `customers.total_spent` (denormalized lifetime, refunds excluded) and zero-spend customers are excluded so trial-only walk-ins don't dominate the <$25 bucket. Auto-hides when fewer than 10 customers have any spend (insufficient signal on fresh installs). Lives between the top-customers card and the refund trend card on Reports. Pure JS, no migration. Closes the "where does my customer base actually sit on the spend curve?" BI gap that the existing top-list (named individuals) and avg-spend-per-visit (visit-level) cards weren't answering.
- **POS: quick-create customer — beefed up — DONE (2026-05-09).** The existing `quickAddCustomer` modal (opened by the user-plus button next to the customer dropdown) was minimal — name / phone / email / city only. Two real ergonomics gaps: (1) **No DOB capture** meant minor-flag, age-gated logic, waiver expiry tracking, and birthday greetings all started broken until owner edited the customer later. (2) **Post-save flow rebuilt the entire customers dropdown from scratch**, dropping any in-flight customer-search filter the cashier had typed AND **didn't fire any of the post-pick refresh hooks** — so the loyalty pill, industry-discount, tax-exempt status, photo thumbnail, notes panel, last-purchase hint, and recent-customer chips all stayed stale until the cashier manually changed and re-changed the dropdown. Now: modal captures name / phone / email / **DOB / guardian-name / guardian-phone** / city / **paper-waiver-on-hand checkbox**. **Auto-shows the guardian row** when the DOB indicates a minor (<18) — fires both on input change + 50ms post-open in case browser autofills DOB after the modal renders. **Required guardian name for minors** (waiver context, emergency contact). Email format validated client-side (`/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/`) so junk doesn't enter the customers table. **Audit-stamps** `[Quick-added YYYY-MM-DD by ACTOR via POS quick-add]` to the customer's notes for traceability — anyone re-opening the customer detail later sees this was a mid-sale capture. **Server returns the new row** (via `Prefer: return=representation`) so we get the UUID without an extra fetch + name-collision lookup. **Local cache update is O(1)** (push + sort) instead of a full reload — keeps the rest of the app instantly aware. Dropdown gets the new option **inserted in alphabetical position** instead of being rebuilt, preserving any in-flight customer-search filter. **All seven post-pick refresh hooks fire** (loyalty / industry-discount / tax-exempt / thumbnail / notes-panel / last-purchase / recent-chips) so every POS surface reflects the new customer immediately. Pure JS, no migration. Closes the cashier ergonomics gap that was forcing cashiers to either skip customer capture entirely OR abandon their cart and rebuild it after creating the customer the long way.
- **Settings: JSON backup &amp; restore — DONE (2026-05-09).** Real disaster-recovery feature for the meaningful amount of config Doug has tuned (tip presets, partner splits, holidays, calendar hours, lesson templates, tag welcome messages, cart presets, instructor payouts, follow-up rules, waiver expiry, renewal-reminder cadence, overdue-rental cadence). Previously a corrupt `app_settings` row or accidental "Reset to defaults" click wiped all of it with no recovery path. New "Settings backup & restore" card on Settings → Data &amp; Backups tab between Data Export and Import Products. **Download** button pulls every `app_settings` row (key='all' + 'followups' + 'renewal_reminders' + 'overdue_rentals' + 'waiver' + any future keys) into one bundle with header metadata (version, timestamp, generated-by email, biz name) + the full in-memory settings object as belt-and-suspenders fallback. JSON-formatted for human readability + filename includes the date so multiple backups don't overwrite (`skateos-settings-backup-2026-05-09.json`). Toast confirms count + size. **Restore** button opens file picker (.json filter), parses the bundle, **validates the magic header** (`__skateos_backup__: 'settings'`, version 1) so corrupt or random JSON can't silently destroy config, shows a confirm dialog with the bundle's metadata + first 10 keys, requires typing **RESTORE (all caps)** as a second-level confirmation, then upserts every row one-at-a-time (so partial failures are visible — toast lists failed keys), restores localStorage as a belt-and-suspenders for the next-paint render, then reloads the page. Multi-row aware so the restore is atomic across all settings keys. Sensitive material (Supabase URL, owner email) is fine in the backup since the file ends up on the user's own computer. Edge Function secrets (Helcim/Resend/Twilio API keys) are NOT in this backup — those live in `supabase secrets`, separate concern. Pure JS, no migration. Closes the irreversible-data-loss gap that's been sitting at zero coverage since launch.

- **Customer detail: likely-duplicate suggest panel — DONE (2026-05-09).** Owner-only inline panel that appears in the customer detail modal when this customer's own email or phone matches another customer record. Auto-hides on no matches OR non-owner viewer (silent in the common case so it doesn't add noise to every customer detail). Pure JS, no migration. Closes the workflow gap where dupe finder was global-only — now the owner can also resolve dupes one at a time as they encounter them in normal customer detail navigation.

Closes a meaningful visibility gap — bus revenue is a real chunk of total revenue but had zero Dashboard surface previously. **Three sections, all conditional**: (1) **Active run banner** — when an active mobile_runs row exists with status='active', renders a rose-tinted pulsing-dot pill with the bus name + how long ago the run started + stats grid (run-to-date gross / sales count / avg ticket — avg only when sales > 0). Configured: 1 bus. Plan a run from Mobile Shop" otherwise. **Auto-hides** when no buses configured (clean for non-mobile installs) OR when no buses + no active run + no inventory (clean even on mobile-enabled installs that haven't started yet). - **Forms: submissions CSV export — DONE (2026-05-09).** Owner-only "Submissions CSV" button on the Forms page header (auto-shows when there's at least one submission). Pass-2 walks submissions to capture ad-hoc keys for forms whose schema changed since the submission landed. Right columns are field answers in schema order. Sorted newest-first so the freshest leads are at the top of the spreadsheet. Multi-line answers collapse to ` · ` separator so each submission stays one row. Object/array values JSON-stringify so embedded structured fields survive. Toast confirms count + field count. Use cases: pull every birthday-party inquiry from the last 30 days into a spreadsheet for follow-up tracking, email all parents who submitted contact-form inquiries about a new program, year-end audit of where leads came from. Body acknowledges the refund amount + reason on file (escaped) + payment-method-aware "where's my money" line: card/Helcim/Venmo → "5-10 business days depending on your bank"; cash → "Stop by the front desk and we\'ll have your $X in cash ready"; comp → "No funds to return — this was a comp\'d sale"; default fallback → "Stop by and we\'ll process in person." Reply-to falls through to bizEmail; bizPhone surfaced when set. Best-effort — email failures log to console and don\'t block the toast (refund is the system of record). Closes the customer-trust gap where refunds previously processed silently and customers had to call to verify. Pure JS, no migration.
- **Mobile bus pre-flight checklist — DONE (2026-05-05).** Settings → Operations → Mobile bus sub-section: free-text checklist editor (one item per line, default 5 items: gear loaded / fuel topped / iPad charged / cash float counted / backup phone). - **Lesson plan templates — DONE (2026-05-05).** Settings → Operations → Lessons sub-section: list editor for `{name, type, body}` templates ("Beginner Camp Day 1", "Intermediate drop-in", "Pro coaching"). Pick a template → `_applyLessonPlanTemplate()` appends `— template name —\n<body>` to existing notes (preserves user-typed notes at the top, doesn't clobber). Idempotency check refuses re-applying the same body twice. Dropdown resets after apply so re-picking the same template works (browser select doesn't fire change on same-value re-pick otherwise). Pure JS — settings round-trip via the existing `app_settings` JSONB. - **Reports: refund rate by product — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Quality signal pairing with the existing re-buy rate card. Async-fetches last 90 days of `sale_items` joined to sales (limit 10000), aggregates per-product sold-qty + refunded-qty + refund rate %. Min 3 units per SKU threshold (lower volume = no signal). Synthetic gift-wrap lines excluded. **3-up headline**: Units sold / Units refunded (red when >0) / Fleet refund rate (color-coded green <2% / amber 2-5% / red ≥5%). **Quality concerns table** when any SKU has ≥10% rate AND ≥1 refund: name + SKU + brand + sold + refunded count + refund % + lost revenue (refunded × avg price). Amber callout below: "⚠ These SKUs have ≥10% refund rate. Investigate: defective batch, sizing issues, expectation mismatch, training gap." **Strong performers table** for SKUs with 0% refunds AND ≥10 sold — useful for marketing testimonials + reorder confidence. Pure JS, no migration. Drives QC conversations with suppliers + product-description fixes.

Per instructor: $/hr = revenue ÷ duration hours, sorted desc. **Per-row visualization**: name + "mostly camp" topType chip / horizontal teal bar (proportional to top earner) / supporting line "8 lessons · 14.5 hrs · avg $52/lesson · $410 total". - **me.html: lifetime savings + this-year stat tiles — DONE (2026-05-05).** Two new stat-card tiles in the customer self-serve portal dashboard (above the existing Loyalty + Visits tiles): **💰 You've saved** (sums `discount` from completed sales + loyalty-redemption value via the default 100pts/$1 fallback rate) — auto-hides when total < $1. **📅 This year** (current-year completed-sale total spent + sale count + savings, computed from the recent_sales array the portal_summary RPC returns) — auto-hides when no sales this year. - **Reports: weekly revenue snapshot — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Bridges the existing 30-day daily revenue trend (Dashboard) and 12-month monthly GMV trend (Reports). Async-fetches sales (limit 5000, since global array caps at 100) for the last 12 Mon-Sun weeks. Net revenue = total - refunded_amount; voided excluded. **3-up stat strip**: Last full week (teal, with sale count) / Week-over-week (color-coded green ↑ / red ↓ / gray → with delta % vs prior full week) / 12-week best (with date label). **Bar chart** — 12 vertical bars, current partial week dimmed (40% opacity), labels for first / mid / last + "now" tag on current. Hover any bar for full tooltip ("Apr 15: $1,247 · 8 sales · $50 refunded (current/partial)"). **Auto-callouts**: green "Last week up X% — replicate it" when WoW ≥+25%; red "Down X% — investigate before trend forms" when WoW ≤-25%; 🏆 "Last week was your best week — lock in what you did" when current is the 12-week peak; amber "📉 High volatility — best 2× worst, smooth via reservations/season passes" when range >2×. Pure JS, no migration. Useful BI gap-filler at the right granularity for "is this week tracking ok?".
- **Check-In closing-soon warning — DONE (2026-05-05).** Settings → Operations → Front desk gains a "Closing-soon warning" sub-section: minutes-before-close threshold (default 30, set 0 to disable). New `ciRenderClosingSoon()` reads today's `settings.hours[<dow>].close`, computes minutes until close, shows a banner above the Check-In grid when within the threshold. **Color escalation**: amber 16–30 min "Closing in 25 min — last call for new check-ins, day passes, and lessons" / red ≤15 min same copy / red ≤5 min stronger copy "Closing in 4 min — refuse new check-ins, finish active sessions." Auto-hides outside the window so it doesn't crowd the screen all day. Refreshed every 60s via `setInterval` while Check-In is open; timer cleared in `go()` when navigating away to other pages. Doesn't fire on closed days (the existing closed-day banner takes over). Pure JS, no migration. Closes the "stop accepting day passes 5 minutes before close" front-desk discipline gap.
- **POS gift wrap fee — DONE (2026-05-05).** Settings → Operations → POS sub-section: "Gift wrap fee ($)" input (default 0 = disabled). When fee > 0, POS shows a "🎁 Add gift wrap (+$5)" button under cart actions (alongside Customer view / Sell gift card). Click → `addGiftWrapToCart()` adds (or increments) a synthetic line at the configured price. Uses sentinel `product_id='__giftwrap__'` to keep cart math + receipt rendering working without polluting the products table. **Synthetic-line guard** in `finalizeSale`: detects `product_id` starting with `__`, NULLs it on `sale_items` insert (FK to products would fail otherwise), skips inventory + bus-stock mutations. Same guard on the single-item `sales.product_id` assignment. Gift wrap is taxable like any other line (no special tax exemption). Cleared on cart-clear naturally via the existing flow. Pure JS, no migration. Closes the gift-season ask without forcing an awkward "create a Gift Wrap product in Products" workflow.

Designed for drag-to-second-monitor at the front desk so the customer can verify their order before paying. **Two-window sync via `window.postMessage`** — every `renderCart()` call (covers all cart mutations: addToCart / qty / remove / clear / discount / tip / customer change / tax-exempt toggle) pushes a fresh state snapshot. Child window posts a "ready" message back on load so initial sync fires regardless of timing.
