- **Reports: lesson booking lead time — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Async-fetches last 90 days of lessons (limit 2000), filters out block-time placeholders (`[BLOCK · ...]` notes — instructors block themselves zero days out, would skew same-day). Computes lead time = `scheduled_at - created_at` per lesson, strips negative (rebooked old) + crazy outliers. **3-up stat strip**: Average lead (purple, smart-formatted h/d/w/mo) / Median lead (with "half book sooner" sub-line) / Same-day bookings % (red when >40%). **Lead-time distribution histogram** with marketing-relevant buckets: Same day (<24h) red / 1–2 days orange / 3–7 days amber / 1–2 weeks cyan / 2–4 weeks teal / 1+ month purple. Bar widths proportional to busiest bucket, count + % per row. **Auto-callouts**: ⚡ "Customers book on impulse — walk-in capacity + signage matter more than lead-time campaigns" (when same-day >40%); 📅 "X% book 1-7 days ahead — best window for 'this weekend' social posts" (when mid-range ≥50%); 🗓 "X% book 2+ weeks ahead — camp/program signal" (when long-lead ≥25%). Footer disclaimer documents the methodology. Drives concrete marketing-cadence + capacity decisions.
- **Settings: Holiday closures — DONE (2026-05-05).** Pairs with the per-DOW park hours system shipped earlier. New `settings.holidays` array of `{date, name}` overrides the day-of-week schedule for specific dates. Two formats accepted: **`YYYY-MM-DD`** (one-time, e.g. "2026-12-25 · Christmas Day" or a one-off ramp resurfacing day) or **`MM-DD`** (recurring annual, e.g. "07-04 · 4th of July"). Settings → Park Hours gains a "Holiday closures" sub-section below the per-day grid: one row per holiday with date + reason inputs + remove button, "Add holiday" button at the bottom. `_parkHoursForDate(yyyy-mm-dd)` checks holidays first (overrides DOW schedule) and returns `{closed:true, holiday:'<name>'}` on match. Existing surfaces auto-pick up the new state: **Lesson modal date warning** shows "🎉 Holiday closure: Christmas Day — verify before booking" instead of the generic closed-day message; **Check-In banner** shows the holiday-specific headline. Pure JS — no migration. Closes the gap between recurring weekly closures and ad-hoc maintenance days.
- **POS hold-cart auto-recover — DONE (2026-05-05).** Every cashier eventually loses a cart to accidental refresh / iPad sleep / browser crash. Now: every cart mutation (`addToCart`, `updateCartQty`, `removeFromCart`, `clearCart`, etc.) auto-saves a draft to `localStorage` (key `skateos_pos_draft`) including cart items + customer + discount + tip + payment method + promo + split-payments + comp reason. Empty carts wipe the draft so stale entries don't pollute storage. **30-min TTL** so a Monday-morning open doesn't restore last Friday's cart. **Recover banner** at top of POS (above held-sales row): "🔄 Recover cart from 12 min ago? · 3 items · $25.50 for Tommy Smith" with Restore + Discard buttons. Auto-shows only when current cart is empty (mid-transaction cashier shouldn't get the prompt). **Restore** path repopulates cart + form fields + global state + recomputes totals + wipes the draft. **Wiped automatically** on successful sale finalization (no need to offer recovery on a completed transaction). Distinct from the existing "Hold sale" feature (explicit named carts) — this is automatic, transient, single-slot. Pure JS — uses `localStorage`, no migration. Universal value, all cashiers benefit.
- **Park-closed-day awareness (Lesson modal + Check-In banner) — DONE (2026-05-05).** Settings → Park Hours has supported per-day open/close + closed-day flagging since launch but the data wasn't surfaced where it mattered. New `_parkHoursForDate(yyyy-mm-dd)` helper returns `{closed, label, hours}` parsing today's day-of-week against `settings.hours[<dow>]`. Wired into two surfaces: (1) **Lesson modal** — date input gains a slot beneath that fires `_lessonDateClosedCheck()` on input. Closed-day picks render a red ⚠ pill ("Park is closed on Mondays — verify before booking"); regular-day picks show a small gray "Park hours: 10:00–18:00" line so cashier sees operating window. Doesn't block save (sometimes a private lesson on a closed day is intentional, e.g. corporate event). Fires once at modal open via the existing setTimeout-after-paint chain. (2) **Check-In screen** — top banner above the grid: red "Park is normally closed on Mondays. Verify with owner before checking skaters in or running sales." Auto-renders at `renderCheckin` if today matches a closed day. Useful catch for the "iPad got powered on for a private booking" scenario where staff might not realize the day is unusual. Pure JS — uses already-existing `settings.hours` storage. Both surfaces fail-closed on missing settings (no banner = no false alarms).
- **Equipment inspection / maintenance tracking — DONE (2026-05-05).** Pure JS overlay on top of `equipment.notes` (no migration). Owner-tunable `settings.equipmentInspectionDays` (default 30 — typical helmet/pad cycle; set to 0 to disable). New `_equipInspectionState(item)` parser reads `[INSPECTED YYYY-MM-DD by NAME]` audit stamps from notes, returns `ok` (green ✓), `soon` (amber ⏰ within 7 days of due), `overdue` (red ⚠), or `never`/`na`/`disabled`. Equipment list rows show a colored inspection pill in the Item cell + the notes preview now strips audit stamps so it's not crowded. **One-click stamp button** (🛡️ teal) per row for in-stock + maintenance items → calls `markEquipmentInspected(id)` which appends the audit line to existing notes. **Bulk inspect** owner-only header button → "Stamp every in-stock item as inspected today?" confirm → batched PATCHes with `[INSPECTED ... · bulk]` marker for the quarterly walk-through scenario. **Dashboard alert chip** "🛡️ N gear items overdue for inspection" surfaces aggressively (matches the safety/insurance significance) with one-click jump to Equipment page. **Settings → Operations → Equipment & safety subgroup** with the interval input + help copy explaining the 30-day default. Real liability protection — when an insurer asks "when did you last inspect this helmet?", the audit trail is in the notes column.
- **Lessons: bulk reschedule — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only "Bulk reschedule" button on Lessons page header (next to Bulk cancel, blue). Substantive ops feature for the snowstorm-makeup-day scenario where moving 8-12 lessons from Saturday to Sunday by individual edit is brutal. Modal: FROM date picker (defaults today, change reloads list), TO date picker (defaults tomorrow), required reason field. Auto-loads list of all `status='scheduled'` lessons matching the FROM date with checkbox per row (default-all-checked, "Select all" toggle), shows time + skater name + instructor + type + price per row. Apply: confirmation prompt, then per-lesson PATCH `scheduled_at` to the new date (preserving original hours/minutes), append `[Rescheduled YYYY-MM-DD → YYYY-MM-DD by NAME: REASON]` to existing notes. After success, **chains to bulk-notify-attendees** with a confirm prompt — "Notify the N rescheduled customer(s) about the new date now?" → opens the bulk-SMS/email modal pre-set to the TO date. Pure JS, no migration. Cancellation-reasons Reports card already parses these stamps so the rescheduling pattern is auditable. Closes the gap between cancel-everything and edit-each-individually for partial-day disruptions.
- **POS: copy receipt to clipboard — DONE (2026-05-05).** Small but high-utility. New 📋 "Copy" button in the Sale Complete modal alongside Email/SMS/Print/Thermal/Re-print. Builds a plain-text receipt using the existing `window._lastReceipt` context (so format stays consistent across all output channels) — biz name + phone + address + receipt # + customer + line items with quantity + serial numbers + subtotal + discount + loyalty redeemed + tax (with EXEMPT label when sale is tax-exempt) + tip + total + payment method + split-payment breakdown when applicable. Copies via `navigator.clipboard.writeText` with a graceful `execCommand('copy')` fallback for older browsers via off-screen textarea. Toast confirms ("Receipt copied to clipboard") or surfaces clear error message. Useful for chargeback disputes, customer chat threads, accounting paste-ins, internal Slack receipts.
- **Reports: lesson cancellation reasons — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Async-fetches last 90 days of cancelled lessons (limit 2000), parses the `[Cancelled YYYY-MM-DD by NAME: REASON]` audit stamps that `cancelLesson` + `bulkCancelLessons` write into lesson notes — including the "by customer (self-serve)" variant from migration 043 + the "(bulk)" tail from bulk cancellations + the fee-applied tail (`weather · 50% fee $25 applied` → "weather"). Buckets reasons via keyword matching: **Weather** (rain/snow/storm/wind/cold/hot), **Instructor unavailable** (sick/out/covid/injur), **Customer-requested** (skater/family/conflict/birthday/reschedul), **Equipment / facility** (broken/repair/maintenance), **Park closure / event** (closure/holiday/private), **No-show (misclassified)** flag for "cancelled" entries that mention no-show, plus **Other** + **(no reason captured)** for blank stamps. Stacked horizontal bar chart (color per bucket), detail table with bucket / count / share% / lost-revenue / top examples per bucket. **Auto-callouts**: ☔ "Weather drives X% — consider rain pass voucher / indoor backup" (when weather ≥40%); amber "Instructor-unavailable is X% — worth backup-pool" (when ≥30%); amber "X% lack a reason — train cashiers" (when unspecified ≥30%); red "N marked cancelled but reason mentions no-show — should be status=no_show, the mig 027 cron handles this" (when noshow_misclass ≥3); 💰 "$X in lost revenue over 90 days, recovering 10% is meaningful". Pure JS, uses already-shipped audit stamps. Closes the "why are we losing lessons?" question with actionable insight.
- **Loyalty bonus points event (multiplier promos) — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-tunable promo days where points earn at a multiplier. Pure JS overlay on top of mig 006's server-side trigger — base earn fires through the trigger, bonus delta fires through a JS hook (`_awardSaleBonusLoyalty` + `_awardCheckinBonusLoyalty`) that inserts a parallel `loyalty_transactions` row with `ref_type='bonus_event_sale'` / `bonus_event_checkin` (distinct from the base earn so the (ref_type, ref_id) UNIQUE INDEX still allows both rows for the same sale_id). Helper `_currentLoyaltyBonus()` reads `settings.loyalty.bonusEvent` and matches by day-of-week OR specific date range (range overrides DOW for one-off promos like "Member Appreciation Week"). **Settings → Operations → Loyalty subgroup**: Active toggle / event name / multiplier (1-10×, half-step) / day-of-week checkbox row (Sun-Sat) / optional date-range inputs. **Surfaces**: WELCOME banner gets a "🎉 2× POINTS" amber pill on check-in days; Loyalty page header gets a full-width gradient banner ("Double Points Tuesday is active today · Sales + check-ins earn 2× points · base earn fires through the trigger, the bonus delta fires from the JS hook") with a "Manage bonus events" jump-to-Settings button for owners. Wired in: finalizeSale's promise chain (after sale insert succeeds) + ciCheckIn (after checkin insert succeeds, fire-and-forget so banner isn't blocked). Best-effort — bonus failures don't block the sale or check-in.
- **Customer detail: insurance claim packet print — DONE (2026-05-05).** New blue "Insurance packet" button in the customer-detail modal footer (next to Print summary). Opens a popup with letter-size print-stylesheet HTML doc auto-firing `window.print()` on load. Pulls everything an insurance adjuster typically asks for, async-fetched on demand: (1) **Skater identification** — name, DOB + age, phone, email, address, customer-since. (2) **Guardian / emergency contact** (only renders for minors) — name, phone, email. - **Reports: product re-buy rate — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Pairs with the re-order shopping list — re-order list answers "what's running low?", this answers "is this product worth re-stocking at all?". Async-fetches last 180 days of `sale_items` joined to completed sales (limit 10000). Per product: counts unique buyers, repeat buyers (≥2 purchases of same SKU), computes re-buy %. **3-up headline**: Overall re-buy rate (green) / Top performers count (blue, ≥30% re-buy + 3+ buyers) / Consider-discontinuing count (amber, <10% re-buy + ≤5 units sold). **Top performers table** sorted by re-buy rate desc — name + SKU + brand + buyer count + repeat-buyer count + re-buy % + units sold + in-stock (color-coded red 0 / amber ≤5 / green, with "⚠ OUT" pill when stocked-out so owner immediately sees "this is a top-performer AND it's out — emergency re-order"). **Discontinue-candidates table** with amber callout suggesting clearance pricing or letting them sell through. Skips walk-in sales (no customer ID to track) + min-3-buyers threshold (lower-volume SKUs lack signal). Memberships/punch cards excluded — "re-buying a 10-pack" is a renewal cycle, not a stocking decision. Footer disclaimer documents both exclusions for transparency.
- **Inventory re-order shopping list — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only "Re-order list" button on Products page header (between Import CSV and Labels). Closes the weekly "what do I order from the distributor?" task. Modal opens with two owner-tunable inputs at top: **lead time (days)** + **safety multiplier** — both recompute the suggested quantities live as the owner types. Async-fetches the last 90 days of `sale_items` (limit 10000, joined with sales filtered to completed/refunded) for accurate per-product velocity, since the global `sales` array is capped at 100. Suggested order qty = `max(threshold × 2, daily_velocity × (lead_days + 30) × safety_mult) - current_stock`, ceil-rounded. Considers **base + bus stock together** (matches dashboard alert chip behavior). Lists every active product at-or-below threshold sorted by velocity desc (urgent items first). Header stat strip: SKU count / estimated cost / "no 90d sales" callout (suggesting discontinue) OR ✓ all-have-velocity. Per-row table: Product (with "0 sales" amber chip when applicable + SKU subtitle) / Brand / Stock (red when 0) / Threshold / 90d sold / Suggested qty (blue, bold) / Cost. **CSV export** with all columns + footer total row, distributor-portal upload-ready. **Print shopping list** opens a popup with letter-size print-stylesheet HTML grouped by brand (distributors typically pack by brand) — header table per brand with Brand name + SKU count + brand subtotal, table rows with SKU code (monospace) + name + stock/threshold + suggested qty (bold blue) + unit price + line cost + checkbox column for marking off as ordered. Footer total + auto-prints on load. Pure JS — no migration. Replaces the spreadsheet-and-Sharpie ritual.

- **Reports: cohort retention heatmap — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Standard SaaS BI pattern: rows = signup-month cohorts (last 8 months), columns = months elapsed (M0/M1/M2…M7), cells = % of cohort active in that month. "Active" defined as **made a purchase OR checked in OR attended a lesson** — not just sales (so members on punch cards aren't penalized for not ringing up new sales mid-pass). BI question.

- **Inventory bulk-import CSV — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only "Import CSV" button on Products page (mirrors the customer-import shipped earlier). Summary line: "ready / skipped / unknown headers ignored". - **Reports: stock-out alert — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Lists active products at 0 stock (sums base `quantity` + bus inventory across all locations so a SKU stocked on the bus isn't false-flagged). Per row: product name + SKU / category + brand / 90-day units sold / last sold relative time / **re-order priority** chip color-coded by velocity (red 🔴 HIGH ≥10 units in 90d, amber 🟠 medium ≥3, gray 🟡 low ≥1, light "no recent sales"). Sorts high-velocity first so the urgent re-orders are at the top. Header surfaces "N of M active products at 0 stock · X%". **Lost-sale-risk callout** auto-fires when ≥1 high-velocity SKU is out: red banner "N high-velocity SKUs are out — these were selling 10+ units / 90 days. Re-order ASAP." Click any row to jump to Products page. Auto-hides when nothing's out (no noise on a fully-stocked install). Truncates list at 50 with overflow count. Pure JS, uses already-loaded `products` + `busInventory` + `sales` arrays.

Long product names truncate at 40 chars. Pure JS using already-loaded `sales` array (capped at 100 globally, but that's plenty for any recent-active customer). - **Lesson modal: recent lesson notes — DONE (2026-05-04).** When the cashier picks a customer who's had previous lessons (in the past, not the one being booked), a collapsible "📖 N past lesson note(s) — click to read" `<details>` section appears below the customer-context hints. - **Reports: refund rate over time — DONE (2026-05-04).** Owner-only Reports card. Last 6 months. Async-fetches sales (status filters: completed + refunded + voided) since global array is capped. Per-month aggregates: total sales count / gross revenue / dollars refunded (full refunds + partials via `refunded_amount` from migration 034) / refund rate %. Renders as a hybrid bar chart where **bar height = sales count, color = refund rate** (green <1% / amber 1-3% / red ≥3%). Detail table below with columns Month / Sales / Gross / Refunded / Refund %. **Spike alert** auto-fires when current month's refund rate is ≥3% AND > 2× last month's: red callout "Spike alert: May refund rate (4.2%) is more than 2× April (1.5%). Investigate — bad batch of product? Staff training gap?" Quality + training-gap canary. Pure JS.

- **Lesson modal: instructor weekly workload hint — DONE (2026-05-05).** Extends the existing instructor-availability hint (On shift now / On staff / New instructor) with a second line showing this-week's scheduled workload: "**This week:** 5 lessons · 12.0 hrs / 25 target". Drives concrete "spread the bookings" decisions when scheduling — cashier sees Doug's already at 35 hrs before assigning him another camp. **Workload math** (`_instructorWeeklyWorkload(name)`): Mon-Sun bucket (Mon-as-start matches payroll convention), counts non-cancelled / non-no-show / non-block-time lessons + sums `duration_min` (defaults 60). **Color coding**: when `staff.weekly_hours_target` is set (mig 008), uses ratio thresholds — green <85% / amber 85-99% / red ≥100% with "(near target)" / "(over target)" stronger labels; falls back to absolute thresholds (35hrs/25hrs/<25hrs red/amber/green) when no target configured. **Open-schedule signal** when picked instructor is on staff with zero lessons booked this week ("Schedule is open") — proactive "this person can take more". Skipped for "New instructor" case (no historical lessons to compute). Pure JS, uses already-loaded lessons + staffList — no DB roundtrip. Closes the over-booking gap that previously required cashier to scroll the calendar to estimate workload.
- **Inventory: bulk discontinue products — DONE (2026-05-05).** Pairs with batch-prices + bulk-import to complete the bulk-product-ops trio. Owner-only red-tinted "Bulk discontinue" button on Products page header. Modal flow: **filter row** (category dropdown / brand dropdown drawn from active SKUs / stock state — Any / Zero only / At-or-below threshold / 90-day sales — Any / None / Fewer than 3) → live matching list with **per-row checkbox default-checked** + Select-all/None controls → required reason. **Smart sort**: zero-stock-no-90d-sales rows surface first (most-likely-dead-stock); secondary sort ascending by 90d sold. **Per-row table** shows product / SKU / brand / total stock (red 0 / orange ≤threshold / gray) / 90d sold (red 0 / orange <3) / cost-tied-up. Live count + dynamic apply-button label ("Discontinue N selected"). **On apply**: PATCHes `products.status='discontinued'` (mig 001 enum value) for each, appends an `inventory_log` row with the bulk-discontinued audit stamp + reason for full trail (the audit_trigger from mig 001 also captures the status change automatically into `audit_log`). **Stock is NOT zeroed** — preserved for accounting; only flips visibility. Local cache updated so the Products page re-renders without the discontinued SKUs after toast confirms count. Reversible via existing product-edit modal (flip status back to active anytime). Pure JS, no migration. Closes the end-of-season cleanup workflow that was previously requiring 30+ individual product edits.
- **Reports: lesson capacity utilization — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Per lesson type (private / group / camp / event / birthday): lesson count, avg booked, avg capacity, **avg utilization %** (booked/capacity), revenue, revenue-per-attendee-slot. Drives concrete capacity + pricing decisions: under-utilized camps need marketing or smaller cap; over-subscribed groups need waitlist + capacity bump; revenue-per-slot gap signals pricing inconsistency. **Booked count math**: solo lessons (max_attendees ≤ 1) count as 1; group/camp/event/birthday count `lesson_attendees` rows with status in (booked, attended, completed) excluding cancelled/no_show/waitlist; falls back to `booked_count` from view (mig 032) or 1 when neither available. Last 90 days of completed (or attended_at-stamped) lessons; block-time placeholders (`[BLOCK ...]` notes) excluded. **4-up stat strip**: Total lessons / Fleet utilization (color-coded green ≥75% / amber 50-74% / red <50%) / Total revenue / Avg per attendee. **Per-type table** with utilization bar chart (color-coded same thresholds), sorted by revenue desc — most economically important type at top. **Auto-callouts** (only fire on multi-attendee types with ≥3 lessons, filters solo-noise): ⚠ "<Type> runs at X% across N sessions — shrink capacity / market push / reprice" (when worst <50%); ⭐ "<Type> running 90%+ full — bump capacity / add slots / raise prices" (when best ≥90%); 💡 "All lessons are solo — pilot group/camp formats to multiply instructor-time revenue" (when no multi-attendee type has ≥3 lessons); 💲 "Per-slot range from $X to $Y — 3×+ spread, check whether lower-price types are pulling weight" (when revenue-per-slot dispersion is wide). Pure JS, uses already-loaded `lessons` + `lessonAttendees` arrays — no DB roundtrip. Lives between Weekend mix card and Discount usage card on the Reports page.
- **Customers: bulk-tag (owner-only) — DONE (2026-05-05).** Closes the "tag 50 winter-camp attendees one at a time" pain point. New "Bulk tag" button on Customers page header (purple-tinted, owner-only). Modal flow: (1) **Source picker** — radio for "Currently filtered list" (defaults selected when an active filter — waiver_expiring / tag:vip / tier:gold / etc — exists; disabled gracefully when no filter) vs "All customers". The filter logic mirrors the existing renderCustomers filter switch so the in-modal count matches what the owner sees on the page. (2) **Operation**: Add tag / Remove tag dropdown. (3) **Tag input** with `<datalist>` autocomplete from the union of all tags currently in use (no schema lookup — pure JS). (4) **Reason** field, required for audit. **Live preview** updates as inputs change: refuses too-long tags (30 char cap), refuses `<>` chars, refuses banned/donotserve aliases via add (forces per-customer Ban button which captures reason + until-date), shows "Will tag N customers · skip M (already tagged)" + first 5 example names. Apply button disabled until preview is actionable. **Idempotent**: rows that already have the tag (when adding) or don't have it (when removing) are skipped. Each modified customer's notes get `[Bulk-tag YYYY-MM-DD by NAME: +<tag> · <reason>]` (or `-` for remove) audit stamp. Series-mode PATCHes (one-at-a-time) so partial failures are visible. Updates local customers cache so the page re-renders with new state immediately. Pure JS, no migration. Use cases: tag winter-camp roster, mark all gold-tier as comp_recipient, sweep an old industry_2024 tag, etc.

New "Status" column between Name and Email surfaces colored chips: 🚫 BANNED (red, highest priority — pulls from `_isBanned()` helper or banned/donotserve/86d tags), ✗ no waiver (red — `ciWaiverState() === 'missing'`, only flagged when total_visits > 0), ⏳ waiver expired (red), ⏳ waiver soon (amber — within 30 days), ⚡ low punches (amber — pre-computed cache from subscriptions array, ≤2 left on active punch_card). **Plus single recency badge** when no higher-priority chip fired (otherwise visual noise): 🆕 new (gray — total_visits=0), 🔥 active (green — visited ≤7d), ⚡ recent (cyan — ≤14d), · Nd ago (slate — ≤30d), 💤 dormant (amber — ≤90d), ❄ lapsed (red — ≤365d), ❄ Ny+ (red — over a year). - **Settings: US federal holidays one-click import — DONE (2026-05-05).** Closes the friction gap on the Holiday closures editor — paste-an-MM-DD-each was tedious for parks just opening or starting fresh. New "+ US federal holidays" button next to the existing "Add holiday" button. Click → confirm prompt → bulk-adds 11 federal holidays as new rows: **5 fixed dates** as `MM-DD` recurring annual entries (New Year's Day, Juneteenth, Independence Day, Veterans Day, Christmas Day) — fire every year automatically; **6 floating dates** computed for current year + next year as one-time `YYYY-MM-DD` entries (MLK Day, Washington's Birthday, Memorial Day, Labor Day, Columbus Day, Thanksgiving) — owner re-clicks next year to extend the floating ones forward. Helpers: `nthWeekdayOf(year, month, dow, n)` for "third Monday in January" calculations + `lastWeekdayOf(year, month, dow)` for Memorial Day's "last Monday in May" pattern. **Idempotent**: reads existing holiday-date inputs from DOM before adding (so unsaved manual edits are preserved) + skips any dates already in the list (case-insensitive trim-aware match) + toasts "All US federal holidays already in list" when nothing to add. Confirm prompt explains the fixed-vs-floating distinction so owner knows to re-click yearly. Toast confirms count + reminds owner to click Save Settings to persist. Pure JS, no migration.
- **Reports: weekend vs weekday revenue mix — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Async-fetches last 90 days of completed-or-refunded sales (limit 10000) since global cap is 100. **Net of refunds** (subtracts `refunded_amount` per mig 034); voided excluded. Buckets revenue + sale count + unique-day-count by day-of-week, then aggregates Weekend (Sat+Sun) vs Weekday (Mon-Fri). **Headline narrative** picks one of 5 labels based on weekend share — "Heavy weekend skew" red 70%+ / "Weekend-leaning" amber 55-69% / "Balanced mix" green 45-54% / "Weekday-leaning" cyan 30-44% / "Heavy weekday skew" purple <30%. **Stacked bar** color-coded purple-on-cyan with hover tooltips per bucket. **4-up stat strip**: Weekend revenue / Weekday revenue / Avg weekend day (revenue ÷ days that had any sale — not skewed by closed days) / Avg weekday. **Per-day-of-week mini chart**: 7 vertical bars, weekend (Sat/Sun) purple + bold-labeled, weekday (Mon-Fri) cyan, height proportional to absolute revenue, hover for details. **Auto-callouts**: ⚠ "70%+ weekend-only — weekend ops + programming matter disproportionately, consider weekday camps/parties to balance" (heavy weekend skew); 💡 "60%+ weekday — unusual for recreation, camp/after-school/industry programs working, double down" (weekday-heavy); 📈 "Weekend day earns 4×+ a weekday — make sure weekend ops are bulletproof" (high lift); ✓ "Weekend earns 2-3× a weekday — healthy recreation ratio, weekday programs pulling weight" (balanced lift); 💡 "Weekday avg > weekend avg — strong weekday signal, keep investing" (inverted lift); 📊 "Best day X 5× slowest day Y — consider reduced hours / private events / close" (large day-spread). Pure JS, no migration. Drives staffing + marketing + scheduling decisions with one glance.

Single-item sales (those with `product_id` set) tally directly from the global sales array. Mirrors the existing Customer / Product / Subscription imports — completes the white-label onboarding suite. Modal accepts file upload OR pasted CSV, parses with the existing `_csvParse` helper (handles quoted fields with embedded commas + escaped quotes), auto-maps headers from common gear export formats: `asset_tag` (or `tag`/`code`/`barcode`/`asset`/`sku`/`asset_id`), `label` (or `name`/`item`/`title`/`product`), `type`, `size`, `status`, `brand`, `notes`. **Loose enum normalization**: `_eqNormalizeType` accepts free-text input ("skateboard" / "deck" / "cruiser" → board, "helm*" → helmet, "knee pad" → pads, "wrist*" / "glove*" → wristguards, "shoe*" / "boot*" / "sneak*" → shoes, fallback → other). Summary line: "X ready / Y skipped / Z unknown headers ignored". Commit batches inserts in chunks of 50, falls back to one-by-one retry if a batch fails to isolate the bad row + collect failing tags for the toast. Pure JS — no migration. Closes the white-label onboarding gap for skateparks importing their loaner inventory from another system or starting from scratch.

- **POS: customer quick-note inline editor — DONE (2026-05-05).** Closes the "I want to capture a thought about this customer mid-transaction without flipping pages" gap. - **Reports: discount usage breakdown — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Pairs with the refund reasons card to complete the "where is money flowing out?" picture (refunds = returns; discounts = give-aways). Async-fetches last 90 days of completed sales with `discount > 0` (limit 5000), plus a parallel fetch of total gross over the same window for "% of gross given away" context. Buckets each sale by source — most-specific first to handle stacked discounts: **Comp / on the house** (`[Comped]` stamp), **Loyalty redemption** (`[Loyalty redeemed]` stamp), **Promo code** (`[Promo code]` stamp OR `promo_code_id` FK NOT NULL), **Industry / sponsored** (`[Industry discount]` stamp OR customer has industry-tag), **Manual / staff discretion** (residual). **Audit stamps amended into `finalizeSale`** at the same time so future sales carry the source attribution: writes `[Loyalty redeemed N pts · -$X]`, `[Promo code CODE applied]`, `[Industry discount auto-applied · -$X]` to `sales.notes` alongside the existing `[Comped]` + `[Tax exempt]` stamps. **4-up stat strip**: Total given (amber) / % of gross (color-coded green <8% / amber 8-15% / red ≥15%) / Avg discount per sale / Top source. **Stacked horizontal bar** by DOLLARS (not count — more honest about cost) with hover tooltips. **Detail table** per source with sales count + total $ + avg/sale + share% + top examples (date + amount + product + customer per row). **Auto-callouts**: 📊 dominant-source narrative ("Loyalty redemption drives 60% of dollars given away — program is doing what it should") with source-specific copy; ⚠ "Manual ≥40% — staff bypass audit trail, coach toward Comp button" (when manual is heavy); ⭐ "Loyalty ≥50% — tune redemption rate if margins suffer"; 🎁 "$X in comps — verify no abuse pattern" (when comp ≥$500); 🚨 "Discounts ≥15% of gross — above industry-typical 5-10%, tightening 5pts = $X annualized" (when over-discounting); ✓ "Discounts only X% — healthy" (when <3%). Footer disclaimer notes that audit stamps were added today, so older discounted sales without stamps bucket as Manual; breakdown sharpens as more post-stamp sales accumulate. Pure JS, no migration. Drives concrete pricing + program-tuning conversations.
- **Sales: void button for cashier mistakes — DONE (2026-05-05).** Distinct from refund: void is for "I rang $50 instead of $5" / "wrong customer" / "double-tapped Complete" — sales that shouldn't have existed. Refund is for legitimate-sale-being-returned. Differences: voids excluded from all reports (status='voided' was already wired throughout the codebase, just no UI to set it before now); no customer confirmation email/SMS (the customer never saw the receipt — it was a misring); time-windowed so it can't be abused to hide bad sales hours later. **Gates**: (a) sale must be `status='completed'`, (b) age within `settings.operations.voidWindowMin` (default 10 min, owner-tunable 1-240 via Settings → Operations → POS subgroup → "Sale void window"), (c) same-cashier (matches `actor_id`) OR owner — staff can void their own mistakes; only owner can void someone else's; legacy pre-actor_id sales unrestricted. **UI**: gray ban-icon button next to the Refund button on Sales History rows + Sale detail modal footer. Auto-hides for ineligible sales — no broken-button experience. **Confirm flow**: dialog explains "VOID is for cashier mistakes / for customer returns use REFUND" + lists what reversing does (status→voided, inventory restored, loyalty reversed via mig 028 trigger). Required reason prompt (audit-stamped to `sales.notes` as `[Voided ISO by NAME: REASON]`). **Inventory restoration**: same logic as full-refund path — handles multi-item sale_items + legacy single-item sales + skips synthetic gift-wrap lines (`__giftwrap__` sentinel). **Loyalty reversal**: free via the mig 028 trigger which fires on `completed → voided` OR `completed → refunded`. Toast confirms "Sale voided · inventory restored · loyalty reversed". Pure JS — no migration needed since the voided status was already part of the schema. Closes the cashier-ergonomics gap that was forcing every misring through the heavier refund flow.
- **Customer detail: outstanding balance card — DONE (2026-05-05).** Surfaces money owed at the per-customer level. Combines two sources: (1) Sales with `payment_method='Pending'` AND status not voided/refunded — these are late-cancel fees, comp-now-pay-later sales, etc. that the existing flows mark Pending so the front desk knows to collect; (2) Unpaid invoices (status `draft`/`sent`/`viewed`/`overdue` from migration 011) — party deposits, custom quotes. Lazy-fetches invoices since they aren't in the global load (silent skip when migration 011 not applied). Subtracts partial refunds (mig 034) from net amounts. **Color escalates** by total: amber <$50, red ≥$50, deep red 🚨 ≥$200. Auto-hides when total < $0.01 (clean for current customers). Renders as a colored card with: header line ("⚠️ Outstanding balance: $X" + N open lines), table with date / source pill (rose-bordered SALE #N or color-coded INV STATUS) / description / amount / Action button. **Per-row action**: pending sales get a "Collect" button → prompts for payment method (numbered list 1-6 default methods + custom override), audit-stamps `[Collected ISO by NAME: payment_method X]` to sales.notes, refreshes the customer detail in place. Invoices get a "View" button → jumps to Invoices page + auto-scrolls to the row. **Bulk action** when ≥2 pending sales and viewer is owner: "Collect all $X" button — single payment-method prompt applies the same method to every pending sale with `(bulk)` audit-stamp tail. Tolerant of partial failure (toast counts both successes + failures). Footer note clarifies what Pending status means. Pure JS, uses already-loaded `sales` array + lazy invoice fetch. Closes the "does this customer owe us anything?" front-desk question without making the cashier scroll the purchase history hunting for Pending rows.
- **Reports: refund reasons breakdown — DONE (2026-05-05).** Owner-only Reports card. Pairs with the existing Lesson cancellation reasons card + Refund rate by product card + Refund rate over time card to complete the "why are we losing money?" picture (this one answers WHY, the others answer WHICH SKUs and WHEN). Async-fetches last 90 days of sales with refunds (`status='refunded'` OR `refunded_amount > 0`, limit 2000) since the global sales array is capped at 100. Parses both refund stamp formats from `sales.notes` written by `refundSale()`: `[Refunded ISO by NAME: REASON]` (full) and `[Partial refund $X on ISO by NAME: REASON]` (partial), takes the LAST stamp when multiple exist on one row. Buckets reasons by keyword: **Defective / quality issue** (broken/cracked/snap/bent/warp/fault/peel/tear), **Wrong size / fit** (size/too big/too small/doesn't fit), **Duplicate / double charge** (duplicate/double/twice/2x), **Cashier error** (mistake/accident/wrong customer/wrong card/misring), **Customer dissatisfied** (didn't like/wrong color/changed mind/disappoint), **Injury / safety event** (injur/hurt/fell/crash/incident/allerg) — flagged separately + cross-reference suggestion, **Linked cancellation** (cancel/no-show), **Gift card return**, **Pricing dispute** (overchar/wrong price/coupon), **Test / training row** (test/demo), plus **Other** + **(no reason captured)**. Stacked horizontal bar chart (color per bucket), detail table with bucket / count / share% / refunded $ / top examples (product name + reason snippet). Header surfaces total refund count split into full vs partial + total $ refunded. **Auto-callouts**: ⚠ "Defective drives X% — push supplier on QC" (when defective ≥30%); 📏 "Sizing issues are X% — post sizing chart at register" (when sizing ≥25%); ⚠ "X duplicate-charge refunds — investigate POS double-tap or Helcim retry loop" (when duplicate ≥3); 🎓 "Cashier errors X% — refresher + two-tap confirm on >$50 sales" (when cashier_error ≥20%); ⚠ "X% lack reason — train cashiers to type more than 'n/a'" (when unspecified ≥30%); 🚨 "X refunds mention injury — cross-ref Incidents page (mig 010) for liability records" (when injury ≥1); 💰 "$X refunded over 90 days — even cutting top bucket 30% is meaningful annualized" (when totalRefunded >$1000); ✓ "Low refund volume + no obvious pattern — healthy state" (when <5 refunds + no other callouts fire). - **iPad touch ergonomics polish — DONE (2026-05-06).** Pure CSS bump targeting touch devices regardless of viewport width. Existing `@media(max-width:768px)` did a heavy mobile-app rewrite that only catches phones + iPad mini portrait — newer iPad portraits (820/834) got the desktop layout, slightly cramped + finger-fight prone. This adds: (1) **`@media(pointer:coarse)`** block — fires on touch screens of any size. Bumps min-height to 44px (Apple HIG minimum) on buttons / btn-icons / nav-items / bottom-tabs. Cart qty +/- buttons get min 40×40 padding. Selects / dropdowns get 44px min-height + 16px font-size to disable iOS auto-zoom on focus. Tables marked `tr[onclick]` get extra vertical row padding for touch accuracy. Tap-highlight color softened. (2) **`@media (min-width:769px) and (max-width:900px)`** specifically for iPad portrait — drops sidebar from 240px to 200px, slightly smaller nav-item font, gives content more horizontal breathing room. Pure CSS, no JS, no migration. Closes the iPad ergonomics gap before Doug runs his actual front-desk operations on the device.

Computes mean + standard deviation of days between this customer's completed-sale visits, surfaces a colored panel between the top-products card and the activity timeline. **Color bands**: 🚨 red "Way overdue" when current gap > mean + 2σ AND > 14 days (heavy nudge needed) · ⏰ amber "A bit overdue" when gap > mean + 1σ AND > 7 days · 🔥 green "On schedule" when gap < mean × 0.5 (healthy regular) · 📅 slate "Visit cadence" otherwise (descriptive). Buckets: Cash / Helcim (card) / Credit card / Gift card / Venmo / Zelle / Check / Comp / Pending / unknown — each color-coded. **Stacked horizontal bar** of revenue share + detail table with per-method revenue, share %, **estimated processing fees** (default 2.9% on Helcim/credit-card lines, owner-tunable via `settings.processingFeeRate`). Footer total row + Pareto callout: when card-like share > 70% of revenue, surfaces "$X in estimated processing fees over 90 days — worth shopping rates if you haven't recently." Useful for processing-fee budget conversations + watching the gift-card share grow once cards take off.
- **Split-payment reconcile + sale-detail rendering — DONE (2026-05-04).** Three follow-ups to the split-payment shipment: (1) **Migration 042 amended** with a payments-aware `reconcile_expected(p_date)` override — sums each split-line into the right bucket (cash / helcim / card_manual / **gift_card** / other) while preserving legacy single-payment row behavior. JSON return gains `expected_gift_card`. Cash-vs-card reconciliation now correct even when half the day's sales are splits. (2) **Close-out modal** displays the Gift card bucket (when >0, green) alongside Cash / Helcim / Card / Other — owner sees gift-card redemptions are tracked separately. (3) **Sale detail modal** payment cell now renders "⊞ split ×3" + indented per-line breakdown when `sales.payments` is populated; falls back to single payment_method otherwise. Closes the financial-accuracy gap split-payments would have created.
- **Split-payment POS — DONE (2026-05-04).** Migration `042_split_payments.sql` adds `sales.payments JSONB` (array of `{method, amount, ref?, note?}`) + array-only CHECK constraint + GIN index for "all sales with payment lines" lookups + helper RPC `sum_payments_by_method(sale_id, method)` for reconciliation. Existing `sales.payment_method` column kept as the "primary" line (largest amount) so legacy reports + filters keep working unchanged. **POS UI**: small `⊞ split` link on the Payment dropdown label opens a modal — pre-populates with Cash + Credit Card lines summing to total, "Add line" up to 5 max, "Auto-balance" sets last line = total - sum of others, live "Balanced / $X short / $X over" status. Confirm-on-mismatch when applying. After apply, primary `payment_method` = the method with the largest amount (auto-adds option to dropdown if missing — e.g. Gift Card / Comp / Other). Status pill shows the breakdown: "⊞ split: Gift Card $20 + Cash $12 + Credit Card $8". `_posSplitPayments` resets on `clearCart`. **Receipt rendering** — both in-app modal and email + thermal receipts now show "Payment · split ×3" header followed by indented per-line breakdown. Use case: customer pays with $20 gift card + $30 cash → both lines logged with amounts → reconciliation sums correctly across split + non-split sales. Migration backlog now 006→042 (37 total).
- **Public gift card balance check page — DONE (2026-05-04).** Standalone page at `admin/gift-card.html` — anyone with the code can check their balance without logging in (the code itself is the access token, 12 random digits = 10^12 keyspace). Pre-fills + auto-submits when the URL has `?code=XXXX-XXXX-XXXX` query parameter (so the code-on-receipt link "just works"). Auto-formats input as the user types (inserts hyphens at positions 4 + 8). Clean rose-themed UI matching the brand. Calls a new `gift_card_balance_lookup(p_code)` RPC added to migration 041 — SECURITY DEFINER, GRANT EXECUTE TO anon, returns ONLY balance + original_amount + status + recipient_name + expires_at (no buyer info, no message). Result-card states: found (green, big balance), fully redeemed (gray, "$0.00"), expired (red), cancelled (red), not found (gray). Print/email gift card receipt now includes the public balance URL inline. Email body to recipient also includes "Check balance anytime: <url>". `config.js` `features.giftCards` flipped to `true`. Closes the standard "what's my balance?" UX without making customers call or visit.
- **Daily digest: gift card liability snapshot — DONE (2026-05-04).** `daily-digest` Edge Function now also queries `gift_cards` (sum balance where status in 'issued','partial') + yesterday's `gift_card_transactions` (issue + redeem deltas). Renders a new "🎁 Gift card liability" section in the email between Auto-pilot and Today: Outstanding balance (amber, $ owed) / count of active cards / Sold yesterday (green, +$X) / Redeemed yesterday (red, -$X). - **POS gift cards (sell + redeem) — DONE (2026-05-04).** Substantive revenue feature. Migration `041_gift_cards.sql` creates two tables: `gift_cards` (code, original_amount, balance, status enum issued/partial/redeemed/refunded/expired/cancelled, recipient info, expires_at, multi-tenant) + `gift_card_transactions` (append-only ledger with sale_id link + delta + balance_after + reason enum issue/redeem/refund/adjust/expire/cancel + actor_id). RLS enabled, authenticated read/write, partial indexes for code lookup + status='issued|partial' + customer FK. **Sell flow** — green "Sell gift card" button on POS opens modal: amount + buyer (optional customer link) + recipient name/email + expiry + payment method + message. Generates a 12-digit code formatted as XXXX-XXXX-XXXX (collision check + unique-index safety net). Inserts a sale row + gift_cards row + ledger issue-row in one transaction-ish flow. Then shows a printable gift-card receipt with the code in monospace + email-to-recipient button (Resend if enabled). **Redeem flow** — new "Gift card" input on POS next to Promo code. Type code → validates (not found / fully redeemed / cancelled / expired) → applies `min(balance, cart subtotal)` as discount → shows status pill "$25 applied · card balance $50 (partial)". On finalizeSale: parallel `_posCommitGiftCardRedemption(saleId)` decrements card balance, flips status to 'redeemed' if balance hits 0, writes ledger redeem-row with delta=-applied. clearCart resets the gift-card state. Pre-migration-041 friendly: insert errors surface a clear "Migration 041 not applied yet" toast. **Doug-side: apply migration 041, then sell + redeem flows are immediately usable.** Migration backlog now 006→041 (36 total).

- **Marketing campaign: tag-based segments — DONE (2026-05-03).** Closes the loop on the tag work shipped this session. Marketing campaign segment dropdown now has TWO optgroups: "Built-in segments" (the existing 7 — everyone-with-email, active members, low-punches, lapsed, recent, birthday-month, has-points) AND "Tag-based segments" (one entry per tag in active use, e.g. `Tagged "vip" (12 with email)`). The tag-based list is sourced from the live union across all customers, with usage counts pre-filtered to email-opted-in customers so the count matches what'll actually receive the campaign. **Banned / do_not_serve / 86d tags are explicitly excluded** — they don't appear as a campaign target option AND `_segmentRecipients` rejects them with a "Banned customers cannot be marketing recipients" reason if somehow chosen via URL/state. Pure JS, no migration. Closes "send a discount code to industry comp customers" / "blast a VIP-only event invite" workflows.
- **Customers list filter-by-tag — DONE (2026-05-03).** Pairs with the tag chips just shipped. Two new entry points: (1) **Tag chips on customer detail are now clickable** — clicking the tag text (separate from the × remove button) jumps to a filtered Customers page showing every customer with that tag. (2) **"All tags" dropdown** on the Customers page header, populated from the live union of tags across all customers (with usage counts: "vip (12)"). Owner picks a tag → same filter activates. Reuses the existing `_customerListFilter` global pattern (Dashboard alert chips already use it for waiver_missing / waiver_expiring / low_punches), now extended with a `tag:<name>` format. Yellow filter banner at the top of the list explains the active filter + "Clear filter" button. Auto-clears when navigating away (already handled in `go()`). Pure JS, no migration. Closes the "show me my industry comp customers" / "who are my regulars?" workflow.
- **Customer detail tag chips UI — DONE (2026-05-03).** Tags drive multiple behavioral features (banned, industry-discount, future VIP perks) but the only way to set them was via the customer edit modal's free-text "tags" input. Now: visible chip row on customer detail (replaces the old single-line "tags" display) with color-coded chips by purpose — red for banned/do_not_serve/86d, amber for industry/comp/sponsored, blue for vip/regular/pro, green for staff/family/employee, gray for everything else. Owner-only `×` button on each chip removes the tag (with confirm). Inline `+ vip / + regular / + industry / + staff` quick-add buttons (only show ones not already applied). Generic add-tag input with autocomplete datalist drawn from the union of all existing tags across customers (natural taxonomy — no schema constraint, but discoverable). Tag input normalizes (lowercase + spaces→underscores), caps at 30 chars, blocks `<>` characters. Banned/do_not_serve add+remove paths route through the existing red Ban / green Lift Ban buttons (those capture audit reasons + notes stamps); the chip ✕ refuses and toasts the user toward the right button. Pure JS, no migration.
- **Overdue rental auto-reminders — BUILT (2026-05-03).** Migration `040_overdue_rental_reminders.sql` adds `equipment_loans.overdue_reminder_sent_at TIMESTAMPTZ` + a partial index (open loans with due_at) + a daily pg_cron at 15:00 UTC (~11am ET). Edge Function `send-overdue-rentals` finds open loans where `due_at < now()` (minus configurable `grace_hours`), respects the `min_gap_h` window so the same loan doesn't get pinged twice in one day, looks up the equipment record for type/size/asset_tag in the email body, color-codes the banner by overdue duration (green ≤1d / amber 1-2d / red 3+d), prefers parent_email for minors, respects `email_opt_out_at`. Built-in template includes the biz phone for "call us if you can't make it back today" CTA. Manual single-loan override: POST `{loan_id}` skips grace + min-gap (owner explicitly clicked). Settings → Follow-ups gets a third section "Overdue rental reminders" with master toggle, grace-hours / min-gap-hours numeric inputs, subject + custom body HTML editor with `{{first}} {{biz}} {{biz_phone}} {{item}} {{due_at}} {{overdue}} {{hours_overdue}}` reference. Separate save button writes to `app_settings` row key='overdue_rentals'. "Send now (test)" button. Added to `deploy-functions.sh`. **Needs: apply migration 040 + redeploy Edge Functions.** Pairs with the existing red Dashboard alert chip "🛹 N overdue rental(s)" (which jumps to the Loaners page for in-person follow-up); now there's automated email pressure too.
- **Customer detail "next action" suggestion — DONE (2026-05-03).** New blue suggestion card on customer detail (between the no-show banner and the loyalty actions row). Pure JS analytic that scans the customer's state and surfaces ONE actionable next step with a one-click CTA button. Priority stack: missing/expired waiver (50) → punch card ≤2 left (40) → birthday in next 7 days (35) → membership expires ≤14 days (30) → lapsed 90+ days (25) → 30-90 day gap "schedule a lesson" (15) → no email captured (10). Each action wired to a real endpoint: waiver→`openWaiverHelper`, punch card renewal→jumps to POS pre-selecting customer, birthday→fires `birthday-greetings` Edge Function (or mailto fallback if their bday isn't actually today), expiring membership→fires `send-renewal-reminders` with the new `subscription_id` override, lapsed→sends rose-themed re-engagement email through Resend (or mailto fallback). Card stays silent on healthy regulars (no false-positive nudges). Closes the "what should I do for this customer?" cognitive load gap that hits every front-desk call.

Edge Function `send-renewal-reminders` finds active subscriptions whose `end_date` is within the configured lead window (default 14d, skip if expired), filters by configurable `plan_types` array (default monthly/annual/punch_card — day_pass disabled by default), respects `email_opt_out_at` + `paused_until`, prefers `parent_email` for minors, fires through Resend with `{{first}} {{biz}} {{plan}} {{end_date}} {{when}} {{days_out}} {{renew_url}}` template variables, stamps the row on success. - **Lesson modal: customer's recurring slot pattern hint — DONE (2026-05-03).** Builds on the customer-context hint shipped earlier. When the cashier picks a skater in the New Lesson modal, the hint now ALSO scans their last 5 lessons (any status — cancelled/no-show count too since they still indicate slot preference) and detects the most-frequent (day-of-week, hour) bucket. If the pattern repeats ≥2 times, surfaces a small blue chip: "📅 Pattern: <strong>Sat 2p</strong> (4 of last 5 lessons) · <strong>Use this slot →</strong>". Clicking the link computes the next future occurrence of that DOW (skipping today if today's slot has already passed) and pre-fills the date + time fields. Re-fires the instructor availability hint after applying. Skips the chip when the pattern is unique (first lesson, or every lesson at a different time) to avoid surfacing noise. Pure JS, no migration. Closes the "what time does Tommy usually book?" gap for repeat skaters without making the cashier flip back to the customer detail page.

Sent-by-lesson-type bar chart underneath. "Missed" defined as: attended in window AND no `followup_sent_at` AND lesson is older than the configured `window_max_h+1` (so the cron has had its full chance to fire). Pre-migration-038 friendly: detects when the column is missing and shows a one-line setup hint linking straight to Settings → Follow-ups instead of polluting the dashboard with false zeros.

- **Partial refunds — DONE (2026-05-01).** Migration `034_partial_refunds.sql` adds `sales.refunded_amount` (numeric, default 0), `refunded_at`, `refunded_by`. - **Group-lesson auto-attend on check-in — DONE (2026-05-01).** Closes a gap in migration 032's group flow. `ciCheckIn` previously only auto-stamped attendance via `lessons.attended_at` keyed off `lessons.customer_id` — meaning a kid in a "Saturday Beginner Camp" (linked via `lesson_attendees`, not the parent's customer_id) didn't get auto-marked when they checked in. Now the auto-attend logic does both: (1) solo path flips `lessons.attended_at` as before but skips lessons with `max_attendees > 1`, (2) group path looks up `lesson_attendees` rows for this customer where the parent lesson is in the ±15 min window and status is still 'booked', then PATCHes those rows to `status='attended'` with `attended_via='checkin_auto'`. Best-effort, non-blocking. Migration 027 also amended to flip attendee rows on the no-show sweep alongside the parent lesson row, with a defensive EXCEPTION handler so it works pre-migration-032.

- **Lesson cancellation flow with billing follow-up — DONE (2026-05-01).** New "Cancel" button on the lesson modal (amber, between Delete and Save). Prompts for a reason, flips lesson status to `cancelled`, mirrors the cancellation onto all `lesson_attendees` rows (silent if migration 032 not applied yet), stamps an audit note onto `lessons.notes` (`[Cancelled DATE by NAME: REASON]`). Then opens a "handle billing?" modal that surfaces (a) up to 5 candidate sales from the customer's last 90 days within ±$5 of the lesson price — each with a one-click "Refund this sale" button that calls existing `refundSale()`, and (b) the customer's active punch card (if any) with a "+1 punch back" button that decrements `punches_used` and stamps the subscription notes. Skips the modal entirely when no candidates exist (toast confirms cancel only). Pure JS — no migration. Solves the 3-step "cancel + find sale + refund" flow that was costing front-desk time.

Opens a modal with: header strip (when / actor / action / table / row id) and a 2-column "before / after" table for UPDATE rows showing every changed field with before-value in red on light-red background, after-value in green on light-green background. Catches dropped keys (fields that existed in old but not new). For INSERT shows the created record with all non-null fields highlighted green; for DELETE shows the deleted snapshot in red. JSON values pretty-printed; long strings truncated with ellipsis. Owner can finally answer "what was the price changed FROM?" without poking at the database directly. Pure JS, uses existing audit_log rows.

- **Loyalty refund reversal — DONE (2026-05-01).** Migration `028_loyalty_refund_reversal.sql` closes a financial leak: previously, refunding a sale after the customer had earned points kept those points on the customer record. New trigger `loyalty_reverse_sale()` fires `AFTER UPDATE OF status ON sales` — when status transitions `'completed' → 'refunded' or 'voided'`, looks up the original earn (where ref_type='sales' AND ref_id=sale.id AND delta>0), and inserts a matching negative loyalty_transactions row with `ref_type='sales_refund'` (so the existing `(ref_type, ref_id)` UNIQUE INDEX from migration 006 doesn't conflict). The `loyalty_apply_delta()` trigger from 006 syncs `customers.loyalty_points` automatically on insert, clamped at 0 by `GREATEST(0,...)`. No JS changes needed for the reversal itself — it fires server-side. `refundSale()` toast now says "loyalty points reversed" when the sale had a customer attached. Loyalty page recent-activity table will show the negative `refund` row in red. Edge cases handled: no original earn (loyalty was disabled at sale time) → no-op; subsequent un-refund won't re-award (manual adjust if needed). **Migration must still be applied.**

- **Lesson no-show auto-mark — DONE (2026-04-30 late evening).** Migration `027_lesson_no_shows.sql` adds RPC `mark_lesson_no_shows(p_window_min INT default 30)` that flips lessons where `status = 'scheduled'` AND `attended_at IS NULL` AND `scheduled_at` is between (now - 7 days) and (now - 30 min) → `status = 'no_show'`. The 7-day backstop prevents stale rows from suddenly flipping months later if a site falls behind on closeout. pg_cron schedules it every 15 minutes (`*/15 * * * *`). - **Loyalty → POS cart-line redemption — DONE (2026-04-30 late evening).** Was the priority-5 polish item: redemption was a 5-click flow from customer detail. Now it's inline in the cart. - **Mobile Bus Shop — REWORKED on 2026-04-30 evening (locations are first-class).** Original 017 design treated each run's inventory as a per-run snapshot. Doug clarified the model in two messages: (1) "Any inventory left on bus will still have that location," and (2) "We certainly will have the same item in both locations — Reds Bearings will have both places at the same time some days." So a SKU can be at base AND on the bus simultaneously — each physical unit is in one place, but the SKU isn't constrained to one location. Total stock for a SKU = `products.quantity` + SUM(`bus_inventory`). Migration `018_inventory_locations.sql` implements this. Schema:
  - `inventory_locations` — seeded with "2nd Nature Park (Base)" + "Bus #1"; supports multiple buses
  - `bus_inventory` — running stock per (location, product); persists across runs
  - `inventory_transfers` — append-only log of base↔bus moves
  - `sales.location_id` — non-null when sale drew from a non-base location; trigger `apply_bus_sale_item` decrements bus_inventory
  - `mobile_runs.vehicle_location_id` — links a run to a specific bus
  - RPCs: `transfer_to_bus()` and `transfer_from_bus()` are atomic — decrement source + upsert dest + log
  - `products.quantity` remains the canonical BASE qty (no schema rewrite of POS / inventory_log triggers)

  **Workflow:** Plan run → Load bus (transfer base→bus, persists) → Activate run (sets sticky `_activeMobileRunId`) → Sales auto-tag with `mobile_run_id` AND `location_id`; bus_inventory decrements via trigger; products.quantity NOT touched → Close run (caches gross/tx in mobile_runs row; bus stock stays on bus for next run) → Optional Unload (transfer bus→base for items going back).

  **Admin UI:** Mobile Shop page shows current bus inventory at top (always visible), with "Load bus" + "Unload bus" buttons. Run list below. Run detail modal shows sales-during-run + bus-checklist (what should be on the bus) with an optional physical-count column for variance audit. Sticky banner across all pages when POS is run-tagged. Reports page gets a "Base shop vs Mobile bus" comparison card.
- **POS → Helcim hosted payment link — WIRED (2026-04-29 evening).** `sendPaymentLink()` in admin/index.html now: (1) creates a local `invoices` row + matching `invoice_items` from cart, (2) calls helcim-invoice Edge Function with line items + tax + customer info + `skateos_invoice_id`, (3) shows the returned `hostedPaymentUrl` with Copy / SMS / Email-via-Resend / preview buttons. The Helcim webhook fires `invoice.paid` → updates local invoice status → done. Includes specific error messages when `HELCIM_API_TOKEN` is missing/invalid (tells Doug what to fix). The disabled "Charge via Helcim Terminal" button is now correctly labelled "Smart Terminal (v1.5)" and gated until hardware integration ships. **Gated on real Helcim token — won't actually fire transactions until Doug replaces the placeholder secret.**
- **send-email Edge Function — BUILT (2026-04-29 evening).** `supabase/functions/send-email/index.ts` proxies to **Resend** (skateOS already configured for Resend in Settings → Integrations, unlike BM which uses SendGrid). CORS, validates email format, supports html / text / both, optional reply_to + tags for Resend analytics. Returns `{ ok, id }` on success or detailed error on failure. Added to `deploy-functions.sh`. **Needs: Doug to (1) verify 2ntr.com sending domain at resend.com, (2) `supabase secrets set RESEND_API_KEY=re_xxx`, (3) re-run deploy script.**

8. **Per-tenant Brivo provisioning (white-label Phase 2).** Doug asked 2026-05-15: when a new skatepark signs up for skateOS, they should get their own Brivo cloud-side access system provisioned — not shared with 2nd Nature's. Current state: migration 064 + 4 Edge Functions ship single-account Brivo (BRIVO_* env vars are one set). Three paths to multi-tenant:
   - **A. Brivo Partner Program** — skateOS becomes Brivo Partner, API-provisions sub-accounts per park, we pass billing through. Requires Brivo partnership contract; we're on the hook for park billing. Best long-term white-label.
   - **B. BYO Brivo credentials (Recommended for v2).** Each park has their own Brivo account, pastes API credentials into Settings → Integrations → Brivo. Move BRIVO_* from Supabase secrets to a `tenant_integrations` table (or extend `app_settings.value.brivo` with per-tenant rows). Edge Functions resolve credentials by `tenant_id` per request. Works today, no Brivo partnership needed; matches the pattern Helcim/Smartwaiver/Twilio already use.
   - **C. Brivo OAuth Connect** — park clicks "Connect Brivo" in Settings, OAuth flow stores tokens per-tenant, auto-refreshed. Best UX; requires Brivo to expose OAuth-as-an-app (verify via Brivo docs).
   
   Build order when ready: (1) `tenant_integrations` table or per-tenant `app_settings` rows, (2) Edge Function refactor to read creds by tenant_id, (3) Settings UI form for paste-in creds + test-connection, (4) Bulk-provision flow when a new tenant signs up, (5) phase 3 = OAuth Connect button.
9. **skateOS Vision Box — on-site Frigate + Coral dongle per park (white-label hardware play).** Doug asked 2026-05-15, immediately after per-tenant Brivo (#8): pair the cloud-side access system with an on-site computer-vision box. Architecture: cloud = Supabase + Brivo (per tenant), on-site = a small device shipped to each park running [Frigate](https://frigate.video/) + [Google Coral USB Accelerator](https://coral.ai/products/accelerator/) (~$60 dongle) on a Raspberry Pi 5 / mini PC (~$200-300). Frigate runs object detection locally on RTSP feeds from the park's existing IP cameras; events stream to skateOS via webhook. **What this unlocks in skateOS:**
   - Cross-reference Brivo door grant + person-at-door detection → confirm auto-checkin (mig 064) attached to the correct human + attach photo to checkins row
   - Intrusion detection: person at park door + NO Brivo grant within 5s → red Dashboard alert + push to owner + save clip
   - Live capacity widget: replace manual `maxCapacity` guess with real-time people-count
   - Auto-prompt incident report (mig 010) with photo + clip pre-attached when a person falls hard / extended ground contact
   - After-hours member entry → auto-attach door-grant photo to their access log row (forensics)
   - Helmet detection (custom model, harder — Phase 3.5)
   - Vehicle/parking-lot arrival patterns → staffing data
   
   **Per-park shipping model:** "skateOS Vision Box" — Pi 5 + Coral + preconfigured Frigate image with the park's `tenant_id` + Supabase service_role secret baked into env. Plug into LAN, point Frigate at their cameras, done. No cloud video bandwidth — only event payloads (timestamps + bounding boxes + small thumbnails) traverse the public internet.
   
   **Build order when ready:** (1) Migration adding `frigate_events` table (event_id, camera, label, score, occurred_at, thumbnail_url, raw_payload JSONB) + tenant-scoped RLS; (2) Edge Function `frigate-webhook` (signature-verified, idempotent, cross-references brivo_access_log by ±5s door-grant window); (3) Dashboard widgets (live capacity, recent intrusion alerts); (4) Customer detail + incident report photo attachment surfaces; (5) Vision Box hardware spec doc + Frigate config template + one-time provisioning script (`scripts/build-vision-box.sh` writes the SD card image with tenant secrets); (6) Pre-flight onboarding flow for new tenants ships a unit before opening day.
